class="hlist noprint nowrap" style="text-align:center;border-top: 1px solid #aaa; padding-top: 3px;"><a href="/wiki/Pacific_typhoon_climatology" title="Pacific typhoon climatology">Pacific typhoon seasons</a><br />\n<a href="/wiki/2015_Pacific_typhoon_season" title="2015 Pacific typhoon season">2015</a>, <a href="/wiki/2016_Pacific_typhoon_season" title="2016 Pacific typhoon season">2016</a>, <b>2017</b>, <i><a href="/wiki/2018_Pacific_typhoon_season" class="mw-redirect" title="2018 Pacific typhoon season">2018</a></i>, <i><a href="/wiki/2019_Pacific_typhoon_season" class="mw-redirect" title="2019 Pacific typhoon season">2019</a></i></td>\n</tr>\n</table>\n<p>The <b>2017 Pacific typhoon season</b> is an ongoing event in the annual cycle of <a href="/wiki/Tropical_cyclone" title="Tropical cyclone">tropical cyclone</a> formation, in which tropical cyclones form in the western Pacific Ocean. The season runs throughout 2017, though most tropical cyclones typically <a href="/wiki/Tropical_cyclogenesis" title="Tropical cyclogenesis">develop</a> between May and October. The season\'s first named storm, Muifa, developed on April 25. This season featured the latest occurrence of the first typhoon of the year since <a href="/wiki/1998_Pacific_typhoon_season" title="1998 Pacific typhoon season">1998</a>, with Noru reaching this intensity on July 23.</p>\n<p>The scope of this article is limited to the Pacific Ocean to the north of the <a href="/wiki/Equator" title="Equator">equator</a> between <a href="/wiki/100th_meridian_east" title="100th meridian east">100\xc2\xb0E</a> and the <a href="/wiki/180th_meridian" title="180th meridian">180th meridian</a>. Within the northwestern Pacific Ocean, there are two separate agencies that assign names to tropical cyclones which can often result in a cyclone having two names. The <a href="/wiki/Japan_Meteorological_Agency" title="Japan Meteorological Agency">Japan Meteorological Agency</a>&#160;<small>(JMA)</small> will name a tropical cyclone should it be judged to have 10-minute <a href="/wiki/Maximum_sustained_wind" title="Maximum sustained wind">sustained wind speeds</a> of at least 65&#160;km/h (40&#160;mph) anywhere in the basin. PAGASA assigns unofficial names to tropical cyclones which move into or form as a tropical depression in their area of responsibility, located between 115\xc2\xb0E\xe2\x80\x93135\xc2\xb0E and between 5\xc2\xb0N\xe2\x80\x9325\xc2\xb0N, regardless of whether or not a tropical cyclone has already been given a name by the JMA. Tropical depressions that are monitored by the United States\' <a href="/wiki/Joint_Typhoon_Warning_Center" title="Joint Typhoon Warning Center">Joint Typhoon Warning Center</a>&#160;<small>(JTWC)</small> are given a numerical designation with a "W" suffix.</p>\n<p></p>\n<div id="toc" class="toc">\n<div class="toctitle">\n<h2>Contents</h2>\n</div>\n<ul>\n<li href="#cite_note-TSR_Jul-2">[2]</a></sup></td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>August 8, 2017</td>\n<td>26</td>\n<td>14</td>\n<td>7</td>\n<td>255</td>\n<td><sup id="cite_ref-TSR_Aug_3-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-TSR_Aug-3">[3]</a></sup></td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<th>Other forecasts<br />\nDate</th>\n<th>Forecast<br />\nCenter</th>\n<th colspan="2">Period</th>\n<th>Systems</th>\n<th>Ref</th>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>January 20, 2017</td>\n<td>PAGASA</td>\n<td colspan="2">January&#160;\xe2\x80\x94 March</td>\n<td>1\xe2\x80\x932 tropical cyclones</td>\n<td><sup id="cite_ref-PAG_1_4-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PAG_1-4">[4]</a></sup></td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>January 20, 2017</td>\n<td>PAGASA</td>\n<td colspan="2">April&#160;\xe2\x80\x94 June</td>\n<td>2\xe2\x80\x934 tropical cyclones</td>\n<td><sup id="cite_ref-PAG_1_4-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PAG_1-4">[4]</a></sup></td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>June 26, 2017</td>\n<td>CWB</td>\n<td colspan="2">January 1 \xe2\x80\x94 December 31</td>\n<td>21\xe2\x80\x9325 tropical storms</td>\n<td><sup id="cite_ref-CWB_5-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CWB-5">[5]</a></sup></td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>July 6, 2017</td>\n<td>PAGASA</td>\n<td colspan="2">July \xe2\x80\x94 September</td>\n<td>6\xe2\x80\x939 tropical cyclones</td>\n<td><sup id="cite_ref-PAG_2_6-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PAG_2-6">[6]</a></sup></td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td>July 6, 2017</td>\n<td>PAGASA</td>\n<td colspan="2">October \xe2\x80\x94 December</td>\n<td>3\xe2\x80\x935 tropical cyclones</td>\n<td><sup id="cite_ref-PAG_2_6-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PAG_2-6">[6]</a></sup></td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<th>2017 season</th>\n<th>Forecast<br />\nCenter</th>\n<th>Tropical<br />\ncyclones</th>\n<th>Tropical<br />\nstorms</th>\n<th>Typhoons</th>\n<th>Ref</th>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td><b>Actual activity</b>:</td>\n<td>JMA</td>\n<td>34</td>\n<td>22</td>\n<td>9</td>\n<td></td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td><b>Actual activity</b>:</td>\n<td>JTWC</td>\n<td>27</td>\n<td>21</td>\n<td>9</td>\n<td></td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td><b>Actual activity</b>:</td>\n<td>PAGASA</td>\n<td>17</td>\n<td>12</td>\n<td>3</td>\n<td></td>\n</tr>\n</table>\n<p>During the year, several national meteorological services and scientific agencies forecast how many tropical cyclones, tropical storms, and typhoons will form during a season and/or how many tropical cyclones will affect a particular country. These agencies include the Tropical Storm Risk&#160;<small>(TSR)</small> Consortium of <a href="/wiki/University_College_London" title="University College London">University College London</a>, <a href="/wiki/PAGASA" title="PAGASA">PAGASA</a> and Taiwan\'s <a href="/wiki/Central_Weather_Bureau" title="Central Weather Bureau">Central Weather Bureau</a>. The first forecast of the year was released by PAGASA during January 20, within its seasonal climate outlook for the period January \xe2\x80\x93 June.<sup id="cite_ref-PAG_1_4-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PAG_1-4">[4]</a></sup> The outlook noted that one to two tropical cyclones were expected between January and March, while two to four were expected to develop or enter the Philippine Area of Responsibility between April and June.<sup id="cite_ref-PAG_1_4-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PAG_1-4">[4]</a></sup> During March 23, the <a href="/wiki/Hong_Kong_Observatory" title="Hong Kong Observatory">Hong Kong Observatory</a> predicted that the tropical cyclone season in Hong Kong would be near-normal, with four to seven tropical cyclones coming within 500&#160;km (310&#160;mi) of the territory compared to an average of six, which was revised to six to nine tropical cyclones in August.<sup id="cite_ref-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-7">[7]</a></sup></p>\n<p>On May 5, Tropical Storm Risk (TSR) issued their first forecast for the season, anticipating an activity of slightly above normal with 27 named storms, 17 typhoons and 10 intense typhoons, including an <a href="/wiki/Accumulated_Cyclone_Energy" class="mw-redirect" title="Accumulated Cyclone Energy">Accumulated Cyclone Energy</a> (ACE) of 357.<sup id="cite_ref-TSR_May_1-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-TSR_May-1">[1]</a></sup> On June 26, Taiwan\'s Central Weather Bureau (CWB) predicted a normal season with 21\xe2\x80\x9425 tropical storms developing over the basin, while three \xe2\x80\x94 five systems were expected to affect Taiwan itself.<sup id="cite_ref-CWB_5-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CWB-5">[5]</a></sup> In the same day, the Thai Meteorological Department (TMD) predicted that 2 tropical cyclones would move towards the northern or northeastern parts of Thailand during August or September.<sup id="cite_ref-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-8">[8]</a></sup> On July 6, TSR released their second forecast for the season, reducing the predicted numbers to 25 named storms, 15 typhoons and 7 intense typhoons, with an ACE Index of 250.<sup id="cite_ref-TSR_Jul_2-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-TSR_Jul-2">[2]</a></sup> During the same day, the PAGASA issued their second and final outlook for the season for the period of July \xe2\x80\x93 December, where six to nine were expected to develop or entered their area of responsibility between July and September while three to five were forecast during October to December. During August 8, the TSR released their third and final forecast for the season, slightly raising their forecast named storms to 26, with 14 reaching typhoon intensity and 7 reaching intense typhoon intensity. ACE Indices were slightly raised to 255.<sup id="cite_ref-TSR_Aug_3-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-TSR_Aug-3">[3]</a></sup></p>\n<div style="clear:both;"></div>\n<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Season_summary">Season summary</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2017_Pacific_typhoon_season&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: Season summary">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>\n<center>\n<div class="timeline-wrapper"><map name="timeline_cb07c0398bda7f9ca37679f941ce154e" id="timeline_cb07c0398bda7f9ca37679f941ce154e">\n<area shape="rect" href="/wiki/Typhoon_Lan_(2017)" coords="623,62,676,83" title="Typhoon Lan (2017)" alt="Typhoon Lan (2017)" />\n<area shape="rect" href="/wiki/Tropical_Depression_23W_(2017)" coords="596,36,648,56" title="Tropical Depression 23W (2017)" alt="Tropical Depression 23W (2017)" />\n<area shape="rect" href="/wiki/Typhoon_Doksuri_(2017)" coords="546,9,621,30" title="Typhoon Doksuri (2017)" alt="Typhoon Doksuri (2017)" />\n<area shape="rect" href="/wiki/Tropical_Storm_Pakhar_(2017)" coords="506,102,576,123" title="Tropical Storm Pakhar (2017)" alt="Tropical Storm Pakhar (2017)" />\n<area shape="rect" href="/wiki/Typhoon_Hato" coords="498,89,556,110" title="Typhoon Hato" alt="Typhoon Hato" />\n<area shape="rect" href="/wiki/Typhoon_Nesat_(2017)" coords="446,22,510,43" title="Typhoon Nesat (2017)" alt="Typhoon Nesat (2017)" />\n<area shape="rect" href="/wiki/Tropical_Storm_Sonca_(2017)" coords="444,182,508,203" title="Tropical Storm Sonca (2017)" alt="Tropical Storm Sonca (2017)" />\n<area shape="rect" href="/wiki/Typhoon_Noru_(2017)" coords="464,156,523,176" title="Typhoon Noru (2017)" alt="Typhoon Noru (2017)" />\n<area shape="rect" href="/wiki/Tropical_Storm_Talas_(2017)" coords="419,142,483,163" title="Tropical Storm Talas (2017)" alt="Tropical Storm Talas (2017)" />\n<area shape="rect" href="/wiki/Tropical_Storm_Nanmadol_(2017)" coords="392,102,472,123" title="Tropical Storm Nanmadol (2017)" alt="Tropical Storm Nanmadol (2017)" /></map><img usemap="#timeline_cb07c0398bda7f9ca37679f941ce154e" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/timeline/cb07c0398bda7f9ca37679f941ce154e.png" /></div>\n</center>\n<p>The <a href="/wiki/Accumulated_Cyclone_Energy" class="mw-redirect" title="Accumulated Cyclone Energy">Accumulated Cyclone Energy</a> for the 2017 Pacific typhoon season, as of 06:00 UTC October 24, is 143.0175&#160;units.<sup id="cite_ref-9" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-9">[nb 1]</a></sup></p>\n<p>The first half of the season was relatively inactive, with only seven systems developing, of which only two intensified into tropical storms. The first system of 2017 developed on January 7, and was named Auring by PAGASA. Tropical Depression Bising developed during the first week of February, and was a factor in, and worsened the effects of, the <a href="/wiki/2017_Visayas_and_Mindanao_floods" title="2017 Visayas and Mindanao floods">2017 Visayas and Mindanao floods</a>. This was followed by Crising, the third system unofficially named by PAGASA. Heavy rains from the depression caused flooding that led to the deaths of 10 people in <a href="/wiki/Cebu" title="Cebu">Cebu</a>, Philippines. Shortly after the dissipation of Crising came the formation of the first tropical storm of the season \xe2\x80\x94 Muifa. The system was not strong, however, and was located away from all major land areas, so it caused no damage. No systems formed during the month of May, the first such occurrence since <a href="/wiki/2013_Pacific_typhoon_season" title="2013 Pacific typhoon season">2013</a>. The next cyclone, Merbok, formed during mid-June, and made landfall in <a href="/wiki/Shenzhen" title="Shenzhen">Shenzhen</a> in China. The cyclone was short-lived; however, it was relatively strong, producing winds of 100&#160;km/h (65&#160;mph) at its peak. Nanmadol passed over the <a href="/wiki/Ryukyu_Islands" title="Ryukyu Islands">Ryukyu Islands</a> and progressed to make landfall in <a href="/wiki/Nagasaki" title="Nagasaki">Nagasaki</a> on Japan\'s island of <a href="/wiki/Kyushu" title="Kyushu">Kyushu</a> during early July. Torrential rainfall and strong winds from the cyclone itself and from the stormy weather that persisted for a number of days were responsible for moderate damage and at least 36 fatalities across mainland Japan.</p>\n<p>By the middle of July, tropical activity had increased with simultaneous tropical storms developing after July 14. Severe Tropical Storm Talas formed during mid-July near the <a href="/wiki/Paracel_Islands" title="Paracel Islands">Paracel Islands</a> in the <a href="/wiki/South_China_Sea" title="South China Sea">South China Sea</a>, and traveled generally westwards. It made landfall in Vietnam after brushing China\'s <a href="/wiki/Hainan" title="Hainan">Hainan</a> province and, unusually, continued to track far inland to the <a href="/wiki/Laos" title="Laos">Laos</a>-<a href="/wiki/Thailand" title="Thailand">Thailand</a> border before weakening to a depression. At least 14 deaths were attributed to the storm, primarily as a result of flooding.</p>\n<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Systems">Systems</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2017_Pacific_typhoon_season&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit section: Systems">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>\n<h3><span id="Tropical_Depression_01W_(Auring)"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Tropical_Depression_01W_.28Auring.29">Tropical Depression 01W (Auring)</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2017_Pacific_typhoon_season&amp;action=edit&amp;section=4" title="Edit section: Tropical Depression 01W (Auring)">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<table class="infobox" style="width:22em;width: 24em;">\n<tr>\n<td colspan="2" style="text-align:center;font-weight: bold; background: #5ebaff">Tropical depression&#160;(JMA)</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td colspan="2" style="text-align:center;font-weight: bold; background: #5ebaff">Tropical depression&#160;(SSHWS)</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td colspan="2" style="text-align:center">\n<div style="vertical-align: middle"><span class="nowrap"><a href="/wiki/File:Auring_2017-01-08_0525z.jpg" class="image"><img alt="Auring 2017-01-08 0525z.jpg" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b5/Auring_2017-01-08_0525z.jpg/150px-Auring_2017-01-08_0525z.jpg" width="150" height="187" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b5/Auring_2017-01-08_0525z.jpg/225px-Auring_2017-01-08_0525z.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b5/Auring_2017-01-08_0525z.jpg/300px-Auring_2017-01-08_0525z.jpg 2x" data-file-width="8353" data-file-height="10433" /></a><span class="nowrap">&#160;</span><a href="/wiki/File:Auring_2017_track.png" class="image"><img alt="Auring 2017 track.png" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/13/Auring_2017_track.png/150px-Auring_2017_track.png" width="150" height="93" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/13/Auring_2017_track.png/225px-Auring_2017_track.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/13/Auring_2017_track.png/300px-Auring_2017_track.png 2x" data-file-width="2700" data-file-height="1669" /></a></span></div>\n</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<th scope="row">Duration</th>\n<td>January 7&#160;\xe2\x80\x93 January 16</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<th scope="row">Peak intensity</th>\n<td>55&#160;km/h (35&#160;mph) <small>(10-min)</small>&#160; 1002&#160;<a href="/wiki/Pascal_(unit)" title="Pascal (unit)">hPa</a>&#160;(<a href="/wiki/Bar_(unit)" title="Bar (unit)">mbar</a>)</td>\n</tr>\n</table>\n<p>On January 7, both PAGASA and the JMA reported that Tropical Depression Auring developed about 400&#160;km (250&#160;mi) to the northeast of <a href="/wiki/Davao_City" title="Davao City">Davao City</a> on <a href="/wiki/Mindanao" title="Mindanao">Mindanao</a>, <a href="/wiki/Philippines" title="Philippines">Philippines</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-10" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-10">[9]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-11" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-11">[10]</a></sup> During that day, the system moved along the southern periphery of a subtropical ridge of high pressure, before the JTWC initiated advisories on the system and designated it as Tropical Depression 01W.<sup id="cite_ref-12" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-12">[11]</a></sup> It later made landfall in the Philippines the next day, and was assessed to have degenerated into a remnant low by the JTWC.<sup id="cite_ref-13" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-13">[12]</a></sup> <span class="citation-needed-content" style="padding-left:0.1em; padding-right:0.1em; color:#595959; border:1px solid #DDD;">The JMA however tracked the system until it emerged into the <a href="/wiki/South_China_Sea" title="South China Sea">South China Sea</a>.</span><sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="margin-left:0.1em; white-space:nowrap;">[<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (May 2017)">citation needed</span></a></i>]</sup> By January 15, the JTWC re-issued advisories as it was located to the east of <a href="/wiki/Vietnam" title="Vietnam">Vietnam</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-14" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-14">[13]</a></sup> However, convection dissipated due to wind shear and land interaction, the JTWC issued their final warnings on January 16.<sup id="cite_ref-15" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-15">[14]</a></sup></p>\n<p>Flooding in <a href="/wiki/Cebu" title="Cebu">Cebu</a> killed one person.<sup id="cite_ref-Auring1_16-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Auring1-16">[15]</a></sup> Damages from Tropical Depression Auring were totaled at <a href="/wiki/Philippine_peso" class="mw-redirect" title="Philippine peso">Ph\xe2\x82\xb1</a>7.14 million (US$140,000) from agriculture and fishing in <a href="/wiki/Negros_Occidental" title="Negros Occidental">Negros Occidental</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-Auring2_17-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Auring2-17">[16]</a></sup></p>\n<div style="clear:both;"></div>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Tropical_Depression_Bising">Tropical Depression Bising</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2017_Pacific_typhoon_season&amp;action=edit&amp;section=5" title="Edit section: Tropical Depression Bising">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<table class="infobox" style="width:22em;width: 24em;">\n<tr>\n<td colspan="2" style="text-align:center;font-weight: bold; background: #5ebaff">Tropical depression&#160;(JMA)</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td colspan="2" style="text-align:center">\n<div style="vertical-align: middle"><span class="nowrap"><a href="/wiki/File:Bising_2017-02-05_0410Z.jpg" class="image"><img alt="Bising 2017-02-05 0410Z.jpg" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/cd/Bising_2017-02-05_0410Z.jpg/150px-Bising_2017-02-05_0410Z.jpg" width="150" height="192" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/cd/Bising_2017-02-05_0410Z.jpg/225px-Bising_2017-02-05_0410Z.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/cd/Bising_2017-02-05_0410Z.jpg/300px-Bising_2017-02-05_0410Z.jpg 2x" data-file-width="6817" data-file-height="8705" /></a><span class="nowrap">&#160;</span><a href="/wiki/File:Bising_2017_track.png" class="image"><img alt="Bising 2017 track.png" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/fa/Bising_2017_track.png/150px-Bising_2017_track.png" width="150" height="93" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/fa/Bising_2017_track.png/225px-Bising_2017_track.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/fa/Bising_2017_track.png/300px-Bising_2017_track.png 2x" data-file-width="2700" data-file-height="1669" /></a></span></div>\n</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<th scope="row">Duration</th>\n<td>February 3&#160;\xe2\x80\x93 February 7</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<th scope="row">Peak intensity</th>\n<td>55&#160;km/h (35&#160;mph) <small>(10-min)</small>&#160; 1000&#160;<a href="/wiki/Pascal_(unit)" title="Pascal (unit)">hPa</a>&#160;(<a href="/wiki/Bar_(unit)" title="Bar (unit)">mbar</a>)</td>\n</tr>\n</table>\n<p>On February 3, a tropical depression developed near <a href="/wiki/Palau" title="Palau">Palau</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-18" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-18">[17]</a></sup> <span class="citation-needed-content" style="padding-left:0.1em; padding-right:0.1em; color:#595959; border:1px solid #DDD;">The system dissipated on the 7th.</span><sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="margin-left:0.1em; white-space:nowrap;">[<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (March 2017)">citation needed</span></a></i>]</sup></p>\n<div style="clear:both;"></div>\n<h3><span id="Tropical_Depression_02W_(Crising)"></span><span class="mw-headline" href="/wiki/Pascal_(unit)" title="Pascal (unit)">hPa</a>&#160;(<a href="/wiki/Bar_(unit)" title="Bar (unit)">mbar</a>)</td>\n</tr>\n</table>\n<table class="plainlinks metadata ambox mbox-small-left ambox-content" role="presentation">\n<tr>\n<td class="mbox-image"><a href="/wiki/File:Wiki_letter_w_cropped.svg" class="image"><img alt="[icon]" //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1c/Wiki_letter_w_cropped.svg/40px-Wiki_letter_w_cropped.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="44" data-file-height="31" /></a></td>\n<td class="mbox-text">\n<div class="mbox-text-span"><b>This section needs expansion</b>. <small>You can help by <a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=2017_Pacific_typhoon_season&amp;action=edit&amp;section=">adding to it</a>.</small> <small><i>(April 2017)</i></small></div>\n</td>\n</tr>\n</table>\n<p>A tropical depression formed over <a href="/wiki/Palau" title="Palau">Palau</a> on April 13.<sup id="cite_ref-19" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-19">[18]</a></sup> During the next 2 days, the system moved toward the Philippines</p>\n<p>As of April 17, at least ten people were reported to be killed in <a href="/wiki/Cebu" title="Cebu">Cebu</a> by flooding caused by the system.<sup id="cite_ref-Crising1_20-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Crising1-20">[19]</a></sup> Total damages throughout the Philippines reached <a href="/wiki/Philippine_peso" class="mw-redirect" title="Philippine peso">Ph\xe2\x82\xb1</a>84.8&#160;million (US$1.7&#160;million), mostly from <a href="/wiki/Danao,_Cebu" title="Danao, Cebu">Danao, Cebu</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-Crising2_21-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Crising2-21">[20]</a></sup></p>\n<div style="clear:both;"></div>\n<h3><span id="Tropical_Storm_Muifa_(Dante)"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Tropical_Storm_Muifa_.28Dante.29">Tropical Storm Muifa (Dante)</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2017_Pacific_typhoon_season&amp;action=edit&amp;section=7" title="Edit section: Tropical Storm Muifa (Dante)">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<table class="infobox" style="width:22em;width: 24em;">\n<tr>\n<td colspan="2" style="text-align:center;font-weight: bold; background: #00faf4">Tropical storm&#160;(JMA)</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td colspan="2" style="text-align:center;font-weight: bold; background: #00faf4">Tropical storm&#160;(SSHWS)</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td colspan="2" style="text-align:center">\n<div style="vertical-align: middle"><span class="nowrap"><a href="/wiki/File:Muifa_2017-04-26_0410Z.jpg" class="image"><img alt="Muifa 2017-04-26 0410Z.jpg" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1f/Muifa_2017-04-26_0410Z.jpg/150px-Muifa_2017-04-26_0410Z.jpg" width="150" height="184" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1f/Muifa_2017-04-26_0410Z.jpg/225px-Muifa_2017-04-26_0410Z.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1f/Muifa_2017-04-26_0410Z.jpg/300px-Muifa_2017-04-26_0410Z.jpg 2x" data-file-width="6609" data-file-height="8100" /></a><span class="nowrap">&#160;</span><a href="/wiki/File:Muifa_2017_track.png" class="image"><img alt="Muifa 2017 track.png" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/45/Muifa_2017_track.png/150px-Muifa_2017_track.png" width="150" height="93" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/45/Muifa_2017_track.png/225px-Muifa_2017_track.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/45/Muifa_2017_track.png/300px-Muifa_2017_track.png 2x" data-file-width="2700" data-file-height="1669" /></a></span></div>\n</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<th scope="row">Duration</th>\n<td>April 22&#160;\xe2\x80\x93 April 29</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<th scope="row">Peak intensity</th>\n<td>65&#160;km/h (40&#160;mph) <small>(10-min)</small>&#160; 1002&#160;<a href="/wiki/Pascal_(unit)" title="Pascal (unit)">hPa</a>&#160;(<a href="/wiki/Bar_(unit)" title="Bar (unit)">mbar</a>)</td>\n</tr>\n</table>\n<p>During April 22, the JMA started to monitor a tropical depression that had developed near <a href="/wiki/Guam" title="Guam">Guam</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-Muifa_BT_22-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Muifa_BT-22">[21]</a></sup> After moving westward for a couple of days, the JTWC began issuing advisories, and designated the storm 03W. By April 25, 03W organized and began consolidating further as the JMA upgraded the depression to a tropical storm, giving it the name <i>Muifa</i>.<sup id="cite_ref-Muifa_BT_22-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Muifa_BT-22">[21]</a></sup> Muifa entered the Philippine Area of Responsibility the following day, and was named <i>Dante</i> by PAGASA.<sup id="cite_ref-23" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-23">[22]</a></sup> The storm, however, started moving northwards and immediately tracked out of the area by April 27. Following this, both the JMA and the JTWC downgraded Muifa to a tropical depression. Muifa fully dissipated early on April 29, and the JMA issued their final advisory on the storm.<sup id="cite_ref-Muifa_BT_22-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Muifa_BT-22">[21]</a></sup></p>\n<div style="clear:both;"></div>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Severe_Tropical_Storm_Merbok">Severe Tropical Storm Merbok</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2017_Pacific_typhoon_season&amp;action=edit&amp;section=8" title="Edit section: Severe Tropical Storm Merbok">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<table class="infobox" style="width:22em;width: 24em;">\n<tr>\n<td colspan="2" style="text-align:center;font-weight: bold; background: #ccffff">Severe tropical storm&#160;(JMA)</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td colspan="2" style="text-align:center;font-weight: bold; background: #00faf4">Tropical storm&#160;(SSHWS)</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td colspan="2" style="text-align:center">\n<div style="vertical-align: middle"><span class="nowrap"><a href="/wiki/File:Merbok_2017-06-12_0506Z.jpg" class="image"><img alt="Merbok 2017-06-12 0506Z.jpg" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/be/Merbok_2017-06-12_0506Z.jpg/150px-Merbok_2017-06-12_0506Z.jpg" width="150" height="204" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/be/Merbok_2017-06-12_0506Z.jpg/225px-Merbok_2017-06-12_0506Z.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/be/Merbok_2017-06-12_0506Z.jpg/300px-Merbok_2017-06-12_0506Z.jpg 2x" data-file-width="5793" data-file-height="7873" /></a><span class="nowrap">&#160;</span><a href="/wiki/File:Merbok_2017_track.png" class="image"><img alt="Merbok 2017 track.png" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/06/Merbok_2017_track.png/150px-Merbok_2017_track.png" width="150" height="93" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/06/Merbok_2017_track.png/225px-Merbok_2017_track.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/06/Merbok_2017_track.png/300px-Merbok_2017_track.png 2x" data-file-width="2700" data-file-height="1669" /></a></span></div>\n</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<th scope="row">Duration</th>\n<td>June 10&#160;\xe2\x80\x93 June 13</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<th scope="row">Peak intensity</th>\n<td>100&#160;km/h (65&#160;mph) <small>(10-min)</small>&#160; 985&#160;<a href="/wiki/Pascal_(unit)" title="Pascal (unit)">hPa</a>&#160;(<a href="/wiki/Bar_(unit)" title="Bar (unit)">mbar</a>)</td>\n</tr>\n</table>\n<p>On June 10, the JMA started to track a tropical depression to the west of <a href="/wiki/Manila" title="Manila">Manila</a>, <a href="/wiki/Philippines" title="Philippines">Philippines</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-Merbok_BT_24-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Merbok_BT-24">[23]</a></sup> After the system entered a region favorable for further development, the depression rapidly organized, prompting the JTWC to start issuing advisories and give it the designation of 04W. A few hours later, 04W had intensified into a tropical storm, receiving the name <i>Merbok</i> as it starts to move in a north-northwestward direction.<sup id="cite_ref-Merbok_BT_24-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Merbok_BT-24">[23]</a></sup> During June 12, Merbok reached its peak intensity with 10-minute winds of 100&#160;km/h (65&#160;mph) and a minimum pressure of 985 hPa, shortly before making landfall in Eastern <a href="/wiki/Shenzen" class="mw-redirect" title="Shenzen">Shenzen</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-Merbok_BT_24-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Merbok_BT-24">[23]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-:0_25-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-:0-25">[24]</a></sup> On June 13, the JMA issued its final warning on Merbok, as the system dissipated over China.<sup id="cite_ref-:0_25-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-:0-25">[24]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Merbok_BT_24-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Merbok_BT-24">[23]</a></sup></p>\n<p>Sustained winds of 51.3 knots (95.0&#160;km/h; 59.0&#160;mph) and a minimum pressure of 990.3&#160;hPa (29.24&#160;inHg) were recorded in <a href="/wiki/Hong_Kong" title="Hong Kong">Hong Kong</a> as the eye passed nearby.<sup id="cite_ref-:0_25-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-:0-25">[24]</a></sup> Across <a href="/wiki/Guangdong_Province" class="mw-redirect" title="Guangdong Province">Guangdong Province</a>, 32&#160;homes were destroyed, 122,000&#160;people reported property damage, and 13,000&#160;hectares of crops flooded. Merbok killed 5 people altogether in Mainland China, 1 from Guangdong and the other 4 were from Hunan.<sup id="cite_ref-Merbok2_26-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Merbok2-26">[25]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Merbok3_27-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Merbok3-27">[26]</a></sup> Total economic losses reached <a href="/wiki/Chinese_yuan" class="mw-redirect" title="Chinese yuan">CN\xc2\xa5</a>516&#160;million (US$76.7&#160;million).<sup id="cite_ref-Merbok1_28-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Merbok1-28">[27]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Merbok2_26-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Merbok2-26">[25]</a></sup></p>\n<div style="clear:both;"></div>\n<h3><span id="Severe_Tropical_Storm_Nanmadol_(Emong)"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Severe_Tropical_Storm_Nanmadol_.28Emong.29">Severe Tropical Storm Nanmadol (Emong)</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2017_Pacific_typhoon_season&amp;action=edit&amp;section=9" title="Edit section: Severe Tropical Storm Nanmadol (Emong)">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<table class="infobox" style="width:22em;width: 24em;">\n<tr>\n<td colspan="2" style="text-align:center;font-weight: bold; background: #ccffff">Severe tropical storm&#160;(JMA)</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td colspan="2" style="text-align:center;font-weight: bold; background: #00faf4">Tropical storm&#160;(SSHWS)</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td colspan="2" style="text-align:center">\n<div style="vertical-align: middle"><span class="nowrap"><a href="/wiki/File:Nanmadol_2017-07-03_0512Z.jpg" class="image"><img alt="Nanmadol 2017-07-03 0512Z.jpg" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d5/Nanmadol_2017-07-03_0512Z.jpg/150px-Nanmadol_2017-07-03_0512Z.jpg" width="150" height="195" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d5/Nanmadol_2017-07-03_0512Z.jpg/225px-Nanmadol_2017-07-03_0512Z.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d5/Nanmadol_2017-07-03_0512Z.jpg/300px-Nanmadol_2017-07-03_0512Z.jpg 2x" data-file-width="2672" data-file-height="3472" /></a><span class="nowrap">&#160;</span><a href="/wiki/File:Nanmadol_2017_track.png" class="image"><img alt="Nanmadol 2017 track.png" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d6/Nanmadol_2017_track.png/150px-Nanmadol_2017_track.png" width="150" height="103" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d6/Nanmadol_2017_track.png/225px-Nanmadol_2017_track.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d6/Nanmadol_2017_track.png/300px-Nanmadol_2017_track.png 2x" data-file-width="2700" data-file-height="1855" /></a></span></div>\n</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<th scope="row">Duration</th>\n<td>July 1&#160;\xe2\x80\x93 July 4</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<th scope="row">Peak intensity</th>\n<td>100&#160;km/h (65&#160;mph) <small>(10-min)</small>&#160; 985&#160;<a href="/wiki/Pascal_(unit)" title="Pascal (unit)">hPa</a>&#160;(<a href="/wiki/Bar_(unit)" title="Bar (unit)">mbar</a>)</td>\n</tr>\n</table>\n<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Tropical_Storm_Nanmadol_(2017)" title="Tropical Storm Nanmadol (2017)">Tropical Storm Nanmadol (2017)</a></div>\n<p>On July 1, the JMA upgraded a low-pressure area it had been monitoring to a tropical depression, located south-southwest of <a href="/wiki/Okinotorishima" title="Okinotorishima">Okinotorishima</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-Nanmadol_BT_29-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Nanmadol_BT-29">[28]</a></sup> Later that day, the JMA began issuing advisories once the depression\'s sustained winds were estimated at 55&#160;km/h (35&#160;mph).<sup id="cite_ref-30" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-30">[29]</a></sup> Shortly thereafter, the PAGASA classified the system as a tropical depression, assigning the local name <i>Emong</i>. On July 2, the JMA classified the system as a tropical storm, and assigned the official name <i>Nanmadol</i>.<sup id="cite_ref-Nanmadol_BT_29-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Nanmadol_BT-29">[28]</a></sup> The JTWC followed suit and gave the internal designation of 05W. The cyclone continued to intensify, and was upgraded by the JMA to a severe tropical storm later that day.<sup id="cite_ref-Nanmadol_BT_29-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Nanmadol_BT-29">[28]</a></sup> Nanmadol reached peak intensity at about 06:00 UTC on July 3,<sup id="cite_ref-Nanmadol_BT_29-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Nanmadol_BT-29">[28]</a></sup> and maintained this strength until making landfall on the western coast of <a href="/wiki/Kyushu" title="Kyushu">Kyushu</a> several hours later. The cyclone began to accelerate while following a generally eastward course across the south of Japan. After brushing the southern coast of <a href="/wiki/Japan" title="Japan">Japan</a>, the JTWC issued its final advisory during the next day. The JMA followed suit late on July 4, when it had become extratropical.<sup id="cite_ref-Nanmadol_BT_29-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Nanmadol_BT-29">[28]</a></sup> Its remnants moved out of the basin three days later.<sup id="cite_ref-Nanmadol_BT_29-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Nanmadol_BT-29">[28]</a></sup></p>\n<p>Evacuation advisories were issued to at least 20,000 residents due to fears of possible flooding and landslides, especially in the prefectures of <a href="/wiki/Niigata_Prefecture" title="Niigata Prefecture">Niigata</a>, <a href="/wiki/Toyama_Prefecture" title="Toyama Prefecture">Toyama</a> and <a href="/wiki/Nagano_Prefecture" title="Nagano Prefecture">Nagano</a>, which had experienced rainfall accumulations of up to 300&#160;mm (12&#160;in) in the preceding hours.<sup id="cite_ref-:2_31-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-:2-31">[30]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-:3_32-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-:3-32">[31]</a></sup> At least three people were injured during the storm\xe2\x80\x94a young boy\'s hand was injured when a school window broke in the city of <a href="/wiki/Kumamoto" title="Kumamoto">Kumamoto</a>, and two adults in Oita prefecture sustained minor injuries after falling due to the strong winds.<sup id="cite_ref-:2_31-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-:2-31">[30]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-:3_32-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-:3-32">[31]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-33" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-33">[32]</a></sup> As of July 13, a total of 30 people have been confirmed dead due to torrential rains which caused landslides and flooding, particularly in <a href="/wiki/Kyushu" title="Kyushu">Kyushu</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-Nanmadol1_34-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Nanmadol1-34">[33]</a></sup></p>\n<div style="clear:both;"></div>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Severe_Tropical_Storm_Talas">Severe Tropical Storm Talas</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2017_Pacific_typhoon_season&amp;action=edit&amp;section=10" title="Edit section: Severe Tropical Storm Talas">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<table class="infobox" style="width:22em;width: 24em;">\n<tr>\n<td colspan="2" style="text-align:center;font-weight: bold; background: #ccffff">Severe tropical storm&#160;(JMA)</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td colspan="2" style="text-align:center;font-weight: bold; background: #00faf4">Tropical storm&#160;(SSHWS)</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td colspan="2" style="text-align:center">\n<div style="vertical-align: middle"><span class="nowrap"><a href="/wiki/File:Talas_2017-07-16_0612Z.jpg" class="image"><img alt="Talas 2017-07-16 0612Z.jpg" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/bd/Talas_2017-07-16_0612Z.jpg/150px-Talas_2017-07-16_0612Z.jpg" width="150" height="200" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/bd/Talas_2017-07-16_0612Z.jpg/225px-Talas_2017-07-16_0612Z.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/bd/Talas_2017-07-16_0612Z.jpg/300px-Talas_2017-07-16_0612Z.jpg 2x" data-file-width="4305" data-file-height="5740" /></a><span class="nowrap">&#160;</span><a href="/wiki/File:Talas_2017_track.png" class="image"><img alt="Talas 2017 track.png" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/cf/Talas_2017_track.png/150px-Talas_2017_track.png" width="150" height="93" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/cf/Talas_2017_track.png/225px-Talas_2017_track.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/cf/Talas_2017_track.png/300px-Talas_2017_track.png 2x" data-file-width="2700" data-file-height="1669" /></a></span></div>\n</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<th scope="row">Duration</th>\n<td>July 14&#160;\xe2\x80\x93 July 17</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<th scope="row">Peak intensity</th>\n<td>95&#160;km/h (60&#160;mph) <small>(10-min)</small>&#160; 985&#160;<a href="/wiki/Pascal_(unit)" title="Pascal (unit)">hPa</a>&#160;(<a href="/wiki/Bar_(unit)" title="Bar (unit)">mbar</a>)</td>\n</tr>\n</table>\n<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Tropical_Storm_Talas_(2017)" title="Tropical Storm Talas (2017)">Tropical Storm Talas (2017)</a></div>\n<p>Early on July 14, the JMA upgraded a low-pressure area in the <a href="/wiki/South_China_Sea" title="South China Sea">South China Sea</a> to a tropical depression after the system began to organize.<sup id="cite_ref-35" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-35">[34]</a></sup> Late the same day, the JMA began issuing advisories on the depression, and forecast it to develop into a tropical storm within the next 24 hours.<sup id="cite_ref-36" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-36">[35]</a></sup></p>\n<p>Talas made landfall near <a href="/wiki/Vinh" title="Vinh">Vinh</a> of <a href="/wiki/Ngh%E1%BB%87_An_Province" title="Ngh\xe1\xbb\x87 An Province">Ngh\xe1\xbb\x87 An Province</a> in <a href="/wiki/Central_Vietnam" title="Central Vietnam">Central Vietnam</a> at 01:00 <a href="/wiki/Indochina_Time" class="mw-redirect" title="Indochina Time">ICT</a> on July 17 (18:00 <a href="/wiki/Coordinated_Universal_Time" title="Coordinated Universal Time">UTC</a> on July 16) as a severe tropical storm.<sup id="cite_ref-37" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-37">[36]</a></sup> In Vietnam, the storm left 14 people dead and damaged around 2,700 houses. A coal ship with 13 crew members sank off the coast of <a href="/wiki/C%E1%BB%ADa_L%C3%B2" title="C\xe1\xbb\xada L\xc3\xb2">C\xe1\xbb\xada L\xc3\xb2</a>, leaving 3 dead and another 3 still unaccounted for.<sup id="cite_ref-38" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-38">[37]</a></sup> Damages reached nearly 1 trillion<a href="/wiki/Vietnamese_dong" class="mw-redirect" title="Vietnamese dong">\xe2\x82\xab</a> (US$43.7 million).<sup id="cite_ref-Talas2_39-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Talas2-39">[38]</a></sup> Despite making landfall in Vietnam, Talas caused a total of CNY 10.89 million(USD 1.64 million) ecomomic losses in Hainan.<sup id="cite_ref-40" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-40">[39]</a></sup></p>\n<div style="clear:both;"></div>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Typhoon_Noru">Typhoon Noru</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2017_Pacific_typhoon_season&amp;action=edit&amp;section=11" title="Edit section: Typhoon Noru">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<table class="infobox" style="width:22em;width: 24em;">\n<tr>\n<td colspan="2" style="text-align:center;font-weight: bold; background: #fdaf9a">Typhoon&#160;(JMA)</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td colspan="2" style="text-align:center;font-weight: bold; background: #ff6060">Category 5&#160;super&#160;typhoon&#160;(SSHWS)</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td colspan="2" style="text-align:center">\n<div style="vertical-align: middle"><span class="nowrap"><a href="/wiki/File:Noru_2017-07-31_0415Z.jpg" class="image"><img alt="Noru 2017-07-31 0415Z.jpg" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/52/Noru_2017-07-31_0415Z.jpg/150px-Noru_2017-07-31_0415Z.jpg" width="150" height="200" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/52/Noru_2017-07-31_0415Z.jpg/225px-Noru_2017-07-31_0415Z.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/52/Noru_2017-07-31_0415Z.jpg/300px-Noru_2017-07-31_0415Z.jpg 2x" data-file-width="4500" data-file-height="6000" /></a><span class="nowrap">&#160;</span><a href="/wiki/File:Noru_2017_track.png" class="image"><img alt="Noru 2017 track.png" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/05/Noru_2017_track.png/150px-Noru_2017_track.png" width="150" height="93" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/05/Noru_2017_track.png/225px-Noru_2017_track.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/05/Noru_2017_track.png/300px-Noru_2017_track.png 2x" data-file-width="2700" data-file-height="1669" /></a></span></div>\n</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<th scope="row">Duration</th>\n<td>July 19&#160;\xe2\x80\x93 August 8</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<th scope="row">Peak intensity</th>\n<td>175&#160;km/h (110&#160;mph) <small>(10-min)</small>&#160; 935&#160;<a href="/wiki/Pascal_(unit)" title="Pascal (unit)">hPa</a>&#160;(<a href="/wiki/Bar_(unit)" title="Bar (unit)">mbar</a>)</td>\n</tr>\n</table>\n<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Typhoon_Noru_(2017)" title="Typhoon Noru (2017)">Typhoon Noru (2017)</a></div>\n<p>The JMA reported that a non-tropical low had transitioned into a tropical depression north-northwest of <a href="/wiki/Wake_Island" title="Wake Island">Wake Island</a> early on July 19.<sup id="cite_ref-41" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-41">[40]</a></sup> Fluctuations in intensity occurred until late on July 29, when <a href="/wiki/Explosive_intensification" class="mw-redirect" title="Explosive intensification">explosive intensification</a> ensued. Damages of agriculture in Wakayama were counted to be JPY 600 million(USD 5.3 million).<sup id="cite_ref-Noru2_42-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Noru2-42">[41]</a></sup></p>\n<div style="clear:both;"></div>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Tropical_Storm_Kulap">Tropical Storm Kulap</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2017_Pacific_typhoon_season&amp;action=edit&amp;section=12" title="Edit section: Tropical Storm Kulap">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<table class="infobox" style="width:22em;width: 24em;">\n<tr>\n<td colspan="2" style="text-align:center;font-weight: bold; background: #00faf4">Tropical storm&#160;(JMA)</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td colspan="2" style="text-align:center;font-weight: bold; background: #00faf4">Tropical storm&#160;(SSHWS)</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td colspan="2" style="text-align:center">\n<div style="vertical-align: middle"><span class="nowrap"><a href="/wiki/File:Kulap_2017-07-24_0230Z_(cropped).jpg" class="image"><img alt="Kulap 2017-07-24 0230Z (cropped).jpg" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/52/Kulap_2017-07-24_0230Z_%28cropped%29.jpg/150px-Kulap_2017-07-24_0230Z_%28cropped%29.jpg" width="150" height="194" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/52/Kulap_2017-07-24_0230Z_%28cropped%29.jpg/225px-Kulap_2017-07-24_0230Z_%28cropped%29.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/52/Kulap_2017-07-24_0230Z_%28cropped%29.jpg/300px-Kulap_2017-07-24_0230Z_%28cropped%29.jpg 2x" data-file-width="363" data-file-height="469" /></a><span class="nowrap">&#160;</span><a href="/wiki/File:Kulap_2017_track.png" class="image"><img alt="Kulap 2017 track.png" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e5/Kulap_2017_track.png/150px-Kulap_2017_track.png" width="150" height="93" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e5/Kulap_2017_track.png/225px-Kulap_2017_track.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e5/Kulap_2017_track.png/300px-Kulap_2017_track.png 2x" data-file-width="2700" data-file-height="1669" /></a></span></div>\n</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<th scope="row">Duration</th>\n<td>July 20&#160;\xe2\x80\x93 July 28</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<th scope="row">Peak intensity</th>\n<td>75&#160;km/h (45&#160;mph) <small>(10-min)</small>&#160; 1002&#160;<a href="/wiki/Pascal_(unit)" title="Pascal (unit)">hPa</a>&#160;(<a href="/wiki/Bar_(unit)" title="Bar (unit)">mbar</a>)</td>\n</tr>\n</table>\n<p>On July 20, the JMA started to monitor a tropical depression that formed over to the southwest of <a href="/wiki/Midway_Atoll" title="Midway Atoll">Midway Atoll</a>, just to the west of the <a href="/wiki/International_Date_Line" title="International Date Line">International Date Line</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-Kulap_BT_43-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Kulap_BT-43">[42]</a></sup> The JTWC classified the system as subtropical, however.<sup id="cite_ref-44" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-44">[43]</a></sup> By July 21, the subtropical storm started to show tropical characteristics, where it prompted both agencies to start issuing advisories, receiving the designation of <i>09W</i> and the name <i>Kulap</i>.<sup id="cite_ref-45" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-45">[44]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Kulap_BT_43-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Kulap_BT-43">[42]</a></sup> During the next day, Kulap briefly reached its peak intensity with 1-minute sustained winds of 95&#160;km/h (60&#160;mph) after imagery depicted some convection over near its compact center.<sup id="cite_ref-46" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-46">[45]</a></sup> After moving westward in a marginally favorable environment, the JMA had reported a minimum pressure of 1002 hPa with peak 10-minute winds of 75&#160;km/h (45&#160;mph) during the early hours of July 24. However several hours later, Kulap had entered in a very unfavorable environment such as cooler waters of 25&#160;\xc2\xb0C (77&#160;\xc2\xb0F).<sup id="cite_ref-47" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-47">[46]</a></sup> Due to strong shear and an <a href="/wiki/Fujiwhara_effect" title="Fujiwhara effect">interaction</a> with Typhoon Noru to its south, Kulap had rapidly weakened; therefore, both agencies issued their final advisory on July 26.<sup id="cite_ref-48" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-48">[47]</a></sup> The JMA, however, tracked Kulap\'s remnants until July 28 when it was absorbed by the outflow of Typhoon Noru.<sup id="cite_ref-Kulap_BT_43-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Kulap_BT-43">[42]</a></sup></p>\n<div style="clear:both;"></div>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Tropical_Storm_Sonca">Tropical Storm Sonca</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2017_Pacific_typhoon_season&amp;action=edit&amp;section=13" title="Edit section: Tropical Storm Sonca">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<table class="infobox" style="width:22em;width: 24em;">\n<tr>\n<td colspan="2" style="text-align:center;font-weight: bold; background: #00faf4">Tropical storm&#160;(JMA)</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td colspan="2" style="text-align:center;font-weight: bold; background: #00faf4">Tropical storm&#160;(SSHWS)</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td colspan="2" style="text-align:center">\n<div style="vertical-align: middle"><span class="nowrap"><a href="/wiki/File:Sonca_2017-07-25_0630Z.jpg" class="image"><img alt="Sonca 2017-07-25 0630Z.jpg" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/77/Sonca_2017-07-25_0630Z.jpg/150px-Sonca_2017-07-25_0630Z.jpg" width="150" height="202" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/77/Sonca_2017-07-25_0630Z.jpg/225px-Sonca_2017-07-25_0630Z.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/77/Sonca_2017-07-25_0630Z.jpg/300px-Sonca_2017-07-25_0630Z.jpg 2x" data-file-width="389" data-file-height="525" /></a><span class="nowrap">&#160;</span><a href="/wiki/File:Sonca_2017_track.png" class="image"><img alt="Sonca 2017 track.png" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/69/Sonca_2017_track.png/150px-Sonca_2017_track.png" width="150" height="93" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/69/Sonca_2017_track.png/225px-Sonca_2017_track.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/69/Sonca_2017_track.png/300px-Sonca_2017_track.png 2x" data-file-width="2700" data-file-height="1669" /></a></span></div>\n</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<th scope="row">Duration</th>\n<td>July 21&#160;\xe2\x80\x93 July 29</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<th scope="row">Peak intensity</th>\n<td>65&#160;km/h (40&#160;mph) <small>(10-min)</small>&#160; 994&#160;<a href="/wiki/Pascal_(unit)" title="Pascal (unit)">hPa</a>&#160;(<a href="/wiki/Bar_(unit)" title="Bar (unit)">mbar</a>)</td>\n</tr>\n</table>\n<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Tropical_Storm_Sonca_(2017)" title="Tropical Storm Sonca (2017)">Tropical Storm Sonca (2017)</a></div>\n<p>On July 21, both the JMA and the JTWC reported that Tropical Depression 08W had developed approximately 582&#160;km (361&#160;mi) to the south of <a href="/wiki/Hong_Kong" title="Hong Kong">Hong Kong</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-Sonca_BT_49-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Sonca_BT-49">[48]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-50" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-50">[49]</a></sup> After moving westward for a couple of days, the system strengthened into a tropical storm by both agencies while nearing the island province of <a href="/wiki/Hainan" title="Hainan">Hainan</a>, receiving the name <i>Sonca</i>.<sup id="cite_ref-51" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-51">[50]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Sonca_BT_49-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Sonca_BT-49">[48]</a></sup> By July 24, Sonca reached its maximum intensity with a minimum pressure of 994 hPa.<sup id="cite_ref-Sonca_BT_49-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Sonca_BT-49">[48]</a></sup> Early on July 25, the JTWC issued its final advisory as the system made landfall over in <a href="/wiki/Qu%E1%BA%A3ng_Tr%E1%BB%8B_Province" title="Qu\xe1\xba\xa3ng Tr\xe1\xbb\x8b Province">Qu\xe1\xba\xa3ng Tr\xe1\xbb\x8b Province</a>, Vietnam.<sup id="cite_ref-52" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-52">[51]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-53" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-53">[52]</a></sup> The JMA issued its final advisory a few hours later when it had weakened into a tropical depression,<sup id="cite_ref-Sonca_BT_49-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Sonca_BT-49">[48]</a></sup> although Sonca maintained its intensity over land until it had fully dissipated on July 29.<sup id="cite_ref-Sonca_BT_49-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Sonca_BT-49">[48]</a></sup></p>\n<p>Flooding in Northern Cambodia drowned two people, blocked many roads and flooded several hundred houses.<sup id="cite_ref-54" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-54">[53]</a></sup> Damage across <a href="/wiki/Sakon_Nakhon" title="Sakon Nakhon">Sakon Nakhon</a>, <a href="/wiki/Thailand" title="Thailand">Thailand</a> exceeded 100&#160;million baht (US$3&#160;million)<sup id="cite_ref-Sonca1_55-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Sonca1-55">[54]</a></sup> and killed 23 people across Thailand.<sup id="cite_ref-56" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-56">[55]</a></sup></p>\n<div style="clear:both;"></div>\n<h3><span id="Tropical_Storm_Roke_(Fabian)"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Tropical_Storm_Roke_.28Fabian.29">Tropical Storm Roke (Fabian)</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2017_Pacific_typhoon_season&amp;action=edit&amp;section=14" title="Edit section: Tropical Storm Roke (Fabian)">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<table class="infobox" style="width:22em;width: 24em;">\n<tr>\n<td colspan="2" style="text-align:center;font-weight: bold; background: #00faf4">Tropical storm&#160;(JMA)</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td colspan="2" style="text-align:center;font-weight: bold; background: #00faf4">Tropical storm&#160;(SSHWS)</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td colspan="2" style="text-align:center">\n<div style="vertical-align: middle"><span class="nowrap"><a href="/wiki/File:Roke_2017-07-22_0600Z.jpg" class="image"><img alt="Roke 2017-07-22 0600Z.jpg" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/6f/Roke_2017-07-22_0600Z.jpg/150px-Roke_2017-07-22_0600Z.jpg" width="150" height="208" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/6f/Roke_2017-07-22_0600Z.jpg/225px-Roke_2017-07-22_0600Z.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/6f/Roke_2017-07-22_0600Z.jpg/300px-Roke_2017-07-22_0600Z.jpg 2x" data-file-width="2047" data-file-height="2834" /></a><span class="nowrap">&#160;</span><a href="/wiki/File:Roke_2017_track.png" class="image"><img alt="Roke 2017 track.png" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/bf/Roke_2017_track.png/150px-Roke_2017_track.png" width="150" height="93" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/bf/Roke_2017_track.png/225px-Roke_2017_track.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/bf/Roke_2017_track.png/300px-Roke_2017_track.png 2x" data-file-width="2700" data-file-height="1669" /></a></span></div>\n</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<th scope="row">Duration</th>\n<td>July 21&#160;\xe2\x80\x93 July 23</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<th scope="row">Peak intensity</th>\n<td>65&#160;km/h (40&#160;mph) <small>(10-min)</small>&#160; 1002&#160;<a href="/wiki/Pascal_(unit)" title="Pascal (unit)">hPa</a>&#160;(<a href="/wiki/Bar_(unit)" title="Bar (unit)">mbar</a>)</td>\n</tr>\n</table>\n<p>The JMA noted the formation of a tropical depression southeast of <a href="/wiki/Taiwan" title="Taiwan">Taiwan</a> early on July 21.<sup id="cite_ref-Roke_BT_57-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Roke_BT-57">[56]</a></sup> Assigning the numerical designation <i>10W</i>, the JTWC upgraded the system to a tropical depression at about 18:00 UTC the same day.<sup id="cite_ref-10W_58-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-10W-58">[57]</a></sup> The system traveled in a generally northwesterly direction, and passed through the <a href="/wiki/Luzon_Strait" title="Luzon Strait">Luzon Strait</a>, between <a href="/wiki/Taiwan" title="Taiwan">Taiwan</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Philippines" title="Philippines">Philippines</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-10W_58-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-10W-58">[57]</a></sup> Around the same time, the PAGASA began issuing advisories on the depression, and contributed the unofficial name <i>Fabian</i>. Early the next day, after the system had emerged into the <a href="/wiki/South_China_Sea" title="South China Sea">South China Sea</a>, both the JMA and the JTWC upgraded the system to a tropical storm, naming it <i>Roke</i>.<sup id="cite_ref-10W_58-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-10W-58">[57]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Roke_BT_57-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Roke_BT-57">[56]</a></sup> Roke assumed a more westerly course, and tracked obliquely towards China\'s <a href="/wiki/Guangdong" title="Guangdong">Guangdong</a> coast.<sup id="cite_ref-:4_59-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-:4-59">[58]</a></sup> The JTWC downgraded the system to a tropical depression just 12 hours later, at 18:00 UTC,<sup id="cite_ref-10W_58-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-10W-58">[57]</a></sup> but the JMA maintained the cyclone\'s category as a tropical storm. Roke made landfall just east of the <a href="/wiki/Hong_Kong" title="Hong Kong">Hong Kong</a> central business district at about 01:30 UTC on July 23, and passed over <a href="/wiki/Shenzhen" title="Shenzhen">Shenzhen</a> one to two hours later.<sup id="cite_ref-:4_59-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-:4-59">[58]</a></sup> Roke weakened to a depression a few hours later, though the JMA declared that it had dissipated on 18:00 UTC of the same day.<sup id="cite_ref-Roke_BT_57-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Roke_BT-57">[56]</a></sup></p>\n<p>Schools, businesses and government offices were closed in Hong Kong as the Hong Kong Observatory (HKO) raised its typhoon warning signal to 8\xe2\x80\x94the third highest of five levels\xe2\x80\x94in preparation for Tropical Storm Roke.<sup id="cite_ref-60" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-60">[59]</a></sup> Ferry services in the city were suspended, and more than 50 flights were delayed.<sup id="cite_ref-61" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-61">[60]</a></sup> However, winds in the city were relatively light and no significant damage was reported.</p>\n<div style="clear:both;"></div>\n<h3><span id="Typhoon_Nesat_(Gorio)"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Typhoon_Nesat_.28Gorio.29">Typhoon Nesat (Gorio)</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2017_Pacific_typhoon_season&amp;action=edit&amp;section=15" title="Edit section: Typhoon Nesat (Gorio)">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<table class="infobox" style="width:22em;width: 24em;">\n<tr>\n<td colspan="2" style="text-align:center;font-weight: bold; background: #fdaf9a">Typhoon&#160;(JMA)</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td colspan="2" style="text-align:center;font-weight: bold; background: #ffffcc">Category 1&#160;typhoon&#160;(SSHWS)</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td colspan="2" style="text-align:center">\n<div style="vertical-align: middle"><span class="nowrap"><a href="/wiki/File:Nesat_2017-07-29_0530Z.jpg" class="image"><img alt="Nesat 2017-07-29 0530Z.jpg" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/0b/Nesat_2017-07-29_0530Z.jpg/150px-Nesat_2017-07-29_0530Z.jpg" width="150" height="200" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/0b/Nesat_2017-07-29_0530Z.jpg/225px-Nesat_2017-07-29_0530Z.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/0b/Nesat_2017-07-29_0530Z.jpg/300px-Nesat_2017-07-29_0530Z.jpg 2x" data-file-width="2100" data-file-height="2800" /></a><span class="nowrap">&#160;</span><a href="/wiki/File:Nesat_2017_track.png" class="image"><img alt="Nesat 2017 track.png" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/40/Nesat_2017_track.png/150px-Nesat_2017_track.png" width="150" height="93" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/40/Nesat_2017_track.png/225px-Nesat_2017_track.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/40/Nesat_2017_track.png/300px-Nesat_2017_track.png 2x" data-file-width="2700" data-file-height="1669" /></a></span></div>\n</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<th scope="row">Duration</th>\n<td>July 25&#160;\xe2\x80\x93 July 30</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<th scope="row">Peak intensity</th>\n<td>150&#160;km/h (90&#160;mph) <small>(10-min)</small>&#160; 960&#160;<a href="/wiki/Pascal_(unit)" title="Pascal (unit)">hPa</a>&#160;(<a href="/wiki/Bar_(unit)" title="Bar (unit)">mbar</a>)</td>\n</tr>\n</table>\n<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Typhoon_Nesat_(2017)" title="Typhoon Nesat (2017)">Typhoon Nesat (2017)</a></div>\n<p>The JMA upgraded a low-pressure area to a tropical depression east of the Philippines early on July 25.<sup id="cite_ref-62" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-62">[61]</a></sup></p>\n<p>Despite the storm not making landfall over in the <a href="/wiki/Philippines" title="Philippines">Philippines</a>, Nesat enhanced the <a href="/wiki/Southwest_monsoon" class="mw-redirect" title="Southwest monsoon">southwest monsoon</a> which brought torrential rainfall over most of the country. As of July 30, the NDRRMC had reported a total of <a href="/wiki/Philippines_peso" class="mw-redirect" title="Philippines peso">Php</a> 105.02 million (US$2.08 million) worth of damages.<sup id="cite_ref-Gorio1_63-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Gorio1-63">[62]</a></sup> Total damages in Taiwan were counted to be NT$60 million(USD 2 million).<sup id="cite_ref-auto_64-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-auto-64">[63]</a></sup> Total damages in Mainland China were counted to be CNY 760 million(USD 114 million).<sup id="cite_ref-auto1_65-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-auto1-65">[64]</a></sup></p>\n<div style="clear:both;"></div>\n<h3><span id="Tropical_Storm_Haitang_(Huaning)"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Tropical_Storm_Haitang_.28Huaning.29">Tropical Storm Haitang (Huaning)</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2017_Pacific_typhoon_season&amp;action=edit&amp;section=16" title="Edit section: Tropical Storm Haitang (Huaning)">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<table class="infobox" style="width:22em;width: 24em;">\n<tr>\n<td colspan="2" style="text-align:center;font-weight: bold; background: #00faf4">Tropical storm&#160;(JMA)</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td colspan="2" style="text-align:center;font-weight: bold; background: #00faf4">Tropical storm&#160;(SSHWS)</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td colspan="2" style="text-align:center">\n<div style="vertical-align: middle"><span class="nowrap"><a href="/wiki/File:Haitang_2017-07-31_0245Z.jpg" class="image"><img alt="Haitang 2017-07-31 0245Z.jpg" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/0e/Haitang_2017-07-31_0245Z.jpg/150px-Haitang_2017-07-31_0245Z.jpg" width="150" height="195" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/0e/Haitang_2017-07-31_0245Z.jpg/225px-Haitang_2017-07-31_0245Z.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/0e/Haitang_2017-07-31_0245Z.jpg/300px-Haitang_2017-07-31_0245Z.jpg 2x" data-file-width="6000" data-file-height="7800" /></a><span class="nowrap">&#160;</span><a href="/wiki/File:Haitang_2017_track.png" class="image"><img alt="Haitang 2017 track.png" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/59/Haitang_2017_track.png/150px-Haitang_2017_track.png" width="150" height="93" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/59/Haitang_2017_track.png/225px-Haitang_2017_track.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/59/Haitang_2017_track.png/300px-Haitang_2017_track.png 2x" data-file-width="2700" data-file-height="1669" /></a></span></div>\n</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<th scope="row">Duration</th>\n<td>July 27&#160;\xe2\x80\x93 August 2</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<th scope="row">Peak intensity</th>\n<td>85&#160;km/h (50&#160;mph) <small>(10-min)</small>&#160; 985&#160;<a href="/wiki/Pascal_(unit)" title="Pascal (unit)">hPa</a>&#160;(<a href="/wiki/Bar_(unit)" title="Bar (unit)">mbar</a>)</td>\n</tr>\n</table>\n<p>A low-pressure area over the northern portion of the South China Sea was upgraded to a tropical depression by the JMA early on July 27.<sup id="cite_ref-66" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-66">[65]</a></sup> Despite an exposed LLCC with disorganized banding, the JTWC started initiating advisories, assigning the designation of <i>12W</i>.<sup id="cite_ref-67" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-67">[66]</a></sup> During the next day, the system had strengthened into a tropical storm, with the JMA naming it as <i>Haitang</i>, after ASCAT image depicted 40 knot winds over in the southern portion of the storm.<sup id="cite_ref-68" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-68">[67]</a></sup> Due to the nearby Typhoon Nesat and moderate wind shear, Haitang maintained its intensity for several hours,<sup id="cite_ref-69" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-69">[68]</a></sup> until on July 30 when the system had deepened and reached its peak intensity with 10-minute sustained winds of 85&#160;km/h (50&#160;mph) with a minimum pressure of 985 hPa. Around the same time, Haitang entered the Philippine area of Responsibility, receiving the name <i>Huaning</i> by PAGASA, although the system had left the area during 12:00 UTC of the same day. Three hours later, the JTWC downgraded the system to a tropical depression,<sup id="cite_ref-70" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-70">[69]</a></sup> though it was re-upgraded into a tropical storm six hours later.<sup id="cite_ref-71" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-71">[70]</a></sup> By July 31, the JTWC issued their final advisory on Haitang after the system had made landfall over in the <a href="/wiki/Pingtan_County" title="Pingtan County">Pingtan County</a> in <a href="/wiki/Taiwan" title="Taiwan">Taiwan</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-72" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-72">[71]</a></sup> <span class="citation-needed-content" style="padding-left:0.1em; padding-right:0.1em; color:#595959; border:1px solid #DDD;">During 06:00 UTC of that day, the JMA issued their final advisory after Haitang weakened into a remnant low.</span><sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="margin-left:0.1em; white-space:nowrap;">[<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (August 2017)">citation needed</span></a></i>]</sup></p>\n<div style="clear:both;"></div>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Tropical_Storm_Nalgae">Tropical Storm Nalgae</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2017_Pacific_typhoon_season&amp;action=edit&amp;section=17" title="Edit section: Tropical Storm Nalgae">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<table class="infobox" style="width:22em;width: 24em;">\n<tr>\n<td colspan="2" style="text-align:center;font-weight: bold; background: #00faf4">Tropical storm&#160;(JMA)</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td colspan="2" style="text-align:center;font-weight: bold; background: #00faf4">Tropical storm&#160;(SSHWS)</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td colspan="2" style="text-align:center">\n<div style="vertical-align: middle"><span class="nowrap"><a href="/wiki/File:Nalgae_2017-08-04_0210Z.jpg" class="image"><img alt="Nalgae 2017-08-04 0210Z.jpg" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/89/Nalgae_2017-08-04_0210Z.jpg/150px-Nalgae_2017-08-04_0210Z.jpg" width="150" height="193" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/89/Nalgae_2017-08-04_0210Z.jpg/225px-Nalgae_2017-08-04_0210Z.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/89/Nalgae_2017-08-04_0210Z.jpg/300px-Nalgae_2017-08-04_0210Z.jpg 2x" data-file-width="5521" data-file-height="7105" /></a><span class="nowrap">&#160;</span><a href="/wiki/File:Nalgae_2017_track.png" class="image"><img alt="Nalgae 2017 track.png" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/29/Nalgae_2017_track.png/150px-Nalgae_2017_track.png" width="150" height="105" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/29/Nalgae_2017_track.png/225px-Nalgae_2017_track.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/29/Nalgae_2017_track.png/300px-Nalgae_2017_track.png 2x" data-file-width="2700" data-file-height="1884" /></a></span></div>\n</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<th scope="row">Duration</th>\n<td>July 31&#160;\xe2\x80\x93 August 5</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<th scope="row">Peak intensity</th>\n<td>85&#160;km/h (50&#160;mph) <small>(10-min)</small>&#160; 990&#160;<a href="/wiki/Pascal_(unit)" title="Pascal (unit)">hPa</a>&#160;(<a href="/wiki/Bar_(unit)" title="Bar (unit)">mbar</a>)</td>\n</tr>\n</table>\n<p>During July 31, the JMA started to monitor a tropical depression located about 1,106&#160;km (687&#160;mi) to the northeast of <a href="/wiki/Wake_Island" title="Wake Island">Wake Island</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-73" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-73">[72]</a></sup> During the next day, the JTWC started issuing advisories and designated it as <i>13W</i>.<sup id="cite_ref-74" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-74">[73]</a></sup> By August 2, both agencies upgraded 13W to Tropical Storm Nalgae after imagery showed flaring convection and the storm was located in a region of low to moderate wind shear and warm SSTs.<sup id="cite_ref-75" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-75">[74]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-76" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-76">[75]</a></sup> Moving in a northward direction, Nalgae slowly intensified for several days. Nalgae reached its peak intensity with 10-minute sustained winds of 85&#160;km/h (55&#160;mph) and a minimum barometric pressure of 988 hPa during August 5 for a brief time, as it was beginning to transition into an extratropical cyclone. The JTWC downgraded Nalgae to a tropical depression later that day and issued their final advisory after the storm was located in very unfavorable environments.<sup id="cite_ref-77" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-77">[76]</a></sup> <span class="citation-needed-content" style="padding-left:0.1em; padding-right:0.1em; color:#595959; border:1px solid #DDD;">The JMA followed suit early on August 6 when Nalgae fully transitioned into an extratropical cyclone, after which its remnants moved further north and were last noted during August 9.</span><sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="margin-left:0.1em; white-space:nowrap;">[<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (August 2017)">citation needed</span></a></i>]</sup></p>\n<div style="clear:both;"></div>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Typhoon_Banyan">Typhoon Banyan</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2017_Pacific_typhoon_season&amp;action=edit&amp;section=18" title="Edit section: Typhoon Banyan">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<table class="infobox" style="width:22em;width: 24em;">\n<tr>\n<td colspan="2" style="text-align:center;font-weight: bold; background: #fdaf9a">Typhoon&#160;(JMA)</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td colspan="2" style="text-align:center;font-weight: bold; background: #ffe775">Category 2&#160;typhoon&#160;(SSHWS)</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td colspan="2" style="text-align:center">\n<div style="vertical-align: middle"><span class="nowrap"><a href="/wiki/File:Banyan_2017-08-15_0148Z.jpg" class="image"><img alt="Banyan 2017-08-15 0148Z.jpg" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/2b/Banyan_2017-08-15_0148Z.jpg/150px-Banyan_2017-08-15_0148Z.jpg" width="150" height="200" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/2b/Banyan_2017-08-15_0148Z.jpg/225px-Banyan_2017-08-15_0148Z.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/2b/Banyan_2017-08-15_0148Z.jpg/300px-Banyan_2017-08-15_0148Z.jpg 2x" data-file-width="2940" data-file-height="3920" /></a><span class="nowrap">&#160;</span><a href="/wiki/File:Banyan_2017_track.png" class="image"><img alt="Banyan 2017 track.png" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/6d/Banyan_2017_track.png/150px-Banyan_2017_track.png" width="150" height="150" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/6d/Banyan_2017_track.png/225px-Banyan_2017_track.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/6d/Banyan_2017_track.png/300px-Banyan_2017_track.png 2x" data-file-width="2700" data-file-height="2700" /></a></span></div>\n</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<th scope="row">Duration</th>\n<td>August 10&#160;\xe2\x80\x93 August 17</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<th scope="row">Peak intensity</th>\n<td>150&#160;km/h (90&#160;mph) <small>(10-min)</small>&#160; 955&#160;<a href="/wiki/Pascal_(unit)" title="Pascal (unit)">hPa</a>&#160;(<a href="/wiki/Bar_(unit)" title="Bar (unit)">mbar</a>)</td>\n</tr>\n</table>\n<table class="plainlinks metadata ambox ambox-content ambox-Unreferenced" role="presentation">\n<tr>\n<td class="mbox-image">\n<div style="width:52px"><a href="/wiki/File:Question_book-new.svg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/9/99/Question_book-new.svg/50px-Question_book-new.svg.png" width="50" height="39" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/9/99/Question_book-new.svg/75px-Question_book-new.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/9/99/Question_book-new.svg/100px-Question_book-new.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="512" data-file-height="399" /></a></div>\n</td>\n<td class="mbox-text">\n<div class="mbox-text-span">This section <b>does not <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citing_sources" title="Wikipedia:Citing sources">cite</a> any <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Verifiability" title="Wikipedia:Verifiability">sources</a></b>. <span class="hide-when-compact">Please help <a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=2017_Pacific_typhoon_season&amp;action=edit">improve this section</a> by <a href="/wiki/Help:Introduction_to_referencing_with_Wiki_Markup/1" title="Help:Introduction to referencing with Wiki Markup/1">adding citations to reliable sources</a>. Unsourced material may be challenged and <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Verifiability#Burden_of_evidence" title="Wikipedia:Verifiability">removed</a>.</span> <small><i>(October 2017)</i></small> <small class="hide-when-compact"><i>(<a href="/wiki/Help:Maintenance_template_removal" title="Help:Maintenance template removal">Learn how and when to remove this template message</a>)</i></small></div>\n</td>\n</tr>\n</table>\n<p><span class="citation-needed-content" style="padding-left:0.1em; padding-right:0.1em; color:#595959; border:1px solid #DDD;">On August 11, a tropical depression had formed. The system then tracked north-west. On August 12th, the systems turned north and underwent intensification (and was named Banyan) until it reached its peak of category 2 at 140km/h (85mp/h) and a pressure of 970 hPa, the storm had not developed an eye wall fully yet. After heading north, the system was disrupted by moderate-strong wind shear caused the system to weaken back to a tropical depression, now tracking north-east. Banyan managed to strengthen again into category 2 (eye did not form here) but was again affected by wind shear and cooler waters, still tracking north-east. Then Banyan headed for Alaska as a tropical storm and before being extra tropical, it dissipated.</span><sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="margin-left:0.1em; white-space:nowrap;">[<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (September 2017)">citation needed</span></a></i>]</sup></p>\n<div style="clear:both;"></div>\n<h3><span id="Typhoon_Hato_(Isang)"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Typhoon_Hato_.28Isang.29">Typhoon Hato (Isang)</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2017_Pacific_typhoon_season&amp;action=edit&amp;section=19" title="Edit section: Typhoon Hato (Isang)">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<table class="infobox" style="width:22em;width: 24em;">\n<tr>\n<td colspan="2" style="text-align:center;font-weight: bold; background: #fdaf9a">Typhoon&#160;(JMA)</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td colspan="2" style="text-align:center;font-weight: bold; background: #ffc140">Category 3&#160;typhoon&#160;(SSHWS)</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td colspan="2" style="text-align:center">\n<div style="vertical-align: middle"><span class="nowrap"><a href="/wiki/File:Hato_2017-08-23_0250Z.jpg" class="image"><img alt="Hato 2017-08-23 0250Z.jpg" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b6/Hato_2017-08-23_0250Z.jpg/150px-Hato_2017-08-23_0250Z.jpg" width="150" height="222" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b6/Hato_2017-08-23_0250Z.jpg/225px-Hato_2017-08-23_0250Z.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b6/Hato_2017-08-23_0250Z.jpg/300px-Hato_2017-08-23_0250Z.jpg 2x" data-file-width="5271" data-file-height="7785" /></a><span class="nowrap">&#160;</span><a href="/wiki/File:Hato_2017_track.png" class="image"><img alt="Hato 2017 track.png" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/0f/Hato_2017_track.png/150px-Hato_2017_track.png" width="150" height="93" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/0f/Hato_2017_track.png/225px-Hato_2017_track.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/0f/Hato_2017_track.png/300px-Hato_2017_track.png 2x" data-file-width="2700" data-file-height="1669" /></a></span></div>\n</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<th scope="row">Duration</th>\n<td>August 19&#160;\xe2\x80\x93 August 24 <small>(<a href="/wiki/2017_North_Indian_Ocean_cyclone_season#Other_systems" title="2017 North Indian Ocean cyclone season">Exited basin</a>)</small></td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<th scope="row">Peak intensity</th>\n<td>140&#160;km/h (85&#160;mph) <small>(10-min)</small>&#160;
