965&#160;<a href="/wiki/Pascal_(unit)" title="Pascal (unit)">hPa</a>&#160;(<a href="/wiki/Bar_(unit)" title="Bar (unit)">mbar</a>)</td>\n</tr>\n</table>\n<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Typhoon_Hato" title="Typhoon Hato">Typhoon Hato</a></div>\n<p>A low-pressure area developed into a tropical depression on August 19 while located to the southeast of <a href="/wiki/Taiwan" title="Taiwan">Taiwan</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-78" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-78">[77]</a></sup></p>\n<p>It gradually intensified and reached typhoon status on the afternoon of August 22 after entering the northeastern part of the South China Sea. On August 23, 07:00 HKT, Hato was approximately 100&#160;km southeast of Hong Kong, bringing rain to the mainland as well as <a href="/wiki/Hainan" title="Hainan">Hainan</a> to the west. At 11:00 HKT the eye was approximately 60&#160;km southwest of Hong Kong with the typhoon heading onto the mainland in a west-northwesterly direction.<sup id="cite_ref-79" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-79">[78]</a></sup></p>\n<p>Hong Kong Observatory issued Hurricane Signal No. 10 at 09:10 HKT, the first time since <a href="/wiki/Typhoon_Vicente" title="Typhoon Vicente">2012</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-80" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-80">[79]</a></sup> A total of 26 people were killed while total damages in South China amounted to CN\xc2\xa512.5 billion (US$1.87 billion).<sup id="cite_ref-Hato1_81-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Hato1-81">[80]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Hato2_82-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Hato2-82">[81]</a></sup> Estimated damages in <a href="/wiki/Hong_Kong" title="Hong Kong">Hong Kong</a> amounted to <a href="/wiki/Hong_Kong_dollar" title="Hong Kong dollar">HK</a>$8 billion (US$1.02 billion).<sup id="cite_ref-Hato3_83-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Hato3-83">[82]</a></sup> In Macau, losses of 11.47 billion patacas (US$1.42 billion) were incurred when high tides exacerbated flooding in most of the lower lying areas, inundating ground floor shops and businesses. There were twelve deaths as a result of the typhoon including a number of people who drowned in flooded underground car-parks.<sup id="cite_ref-Hato4_84-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Hato4-84">[83]</a></sup></p>\n<div style="clear:both;"></div>\n<h3><span id="Severe_Tropical_Storm_Pakhar_(Jolina)"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Severe_Tropical_Storm_Pakhar_.28Jolina.29">Severe Tropical Storm Pakhar (Jolina)</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2017_Pacific_typhoon_season&amp;action=edit&amp;section=20" title="Edit section: Severe Tropical Storm Pakhar (Jolina)">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<table class="infobox" style="width:22em;width: 24em;">\n<tr>\n<td colspan="2" style="text-align:center;font-weight: bold; background: #ccffff">Severe tropical storm&#160;(JMA)</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td colspan="2" style="text-align:center;font-weight: bold; background: #00faf4">Tropical storm&#160;(SSHWS)</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td colspan="2" style="text-align:center">\n<div style="vertical-align: middle"><span class="nowrap"><a href="/wiki/File:Pakhar_2017-08-27_0625Z.jpg" class="image"><img alt="Pakhar 2017-08-27 0625Z.jpg" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d3/Pakhar_2017-08-27_0625Z.jpg/150px-Pakhar_2017-08-27_0625Z.jpg" width="150" height="209" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d3/Pakhar_2017-08-27_0625Z.jpg/225px-Pakhar_2017-08-27_0625Z.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d3/Pakhar_2017-08-27_0625Z.jpg/300px-Pakhar_2017-08-27_0625Z.jpg 2x" data-file-width="2605" data-file-height="3627" /></a><span class="nowrap">&#160;</span><a href="/wiki/File:Pakhar_2017_track.png" class="image"><img alt="Pakhar 2017 track.png" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/37/Pakhar_2017_track.png/150px-Pakhar_2017_track.png" width="150" height="93" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/37/Pakhar_2017_track.png/225px-Pakhar_2017_track.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/37/Pakhar_2017_track.png/300px-Pakhar_2017_track.png 2x" data-file-width="2700" data-file-height="1669" /></a></span></div>\n</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<th scope="row">Duration</th>\n<td>August 24&#160;\xe2\x80\x93 August 28</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<th scope="row">Peak intensity</th>\n<td>100&#160;km/h (65&#160;mph) <small>(10-min)</small>&#160; 985&#160;<a href="/wiki/Pascal_(unit)" title="Pascal (unit)">hPa</a>&#160;(<a href="/wiki/Bar_(unit)" title="Bar (unit)">mbar</a>)</td>\n</tr>\n</table>\n<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Tropical_Storm_Pakhar_(2017)" title="Tropical Storm Pakhar (2017)">Tropical Storm Pakhar (2017)</a></div>\n<p>On August 26, Pakhar passed over the Philippines heading westward toward mainland <a href="/wiki/China" title="China">China</a> where it gathered strength before making landfall in Tianshan on August 27.</p>\n<p>Total economic losses in South China have amounted to CN\xc2\xa5320 million (US$49 million) while a total of eight people have been killed so far as of August 29.<sup id="cite_ref-Pakhar1_85-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Pakhar1-85">[84]</a></sup> Moreover, damages in the <a href="/wiki/Philippines" title="Philippines">Philippines</a> were recorded at PhP41.27 million (US$808 thousand) and 2 billion<a href="/wiki/Vietnamese_dong" class="mw-redirect" title="Vietnamese dong">\xe2\x82\xab</a> (US$85,000) in <a href="/wiki/Vietnam" title="Vietnam">Vietnam</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-Pakhar3_86-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Pakhar3-86">[85]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Pakhar2_87-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Pakhar2-87">[86]</a></sup></p>\n<div style="clear:both;"></div>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Typhoon_Sanvu">Typhoon Sanvu</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2017_Pacific_typhoon_season&amp;action=edit&amp;section=21" title="Edit section: Typhoon Sanvu">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<table class="infobox" style="width:22em;width: 24em;">\n<tr>\n<td colspan="2" style="text-align:center;font-weight: bold; background: #fdaf9a">Typhoon&#160;(JMA)</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td colspan="2" style="text-align:center;font-weight: bold; background: #ffe775">Category 2&#160;typhoon&#160;(SSHWS)</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td colspan="2" style="text-align:center">\n<div style="vertical-align: middle"><span class="nowrap"><a href="/wiki/File:Sanvu_2017-09-01_0105Z.jpg" class="image"><img alt="Sanvu 2017-09-01 0105Z.jpg" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e4/Sanvu_2017-09-01_0105Z.jpg/150px-Sanvu_2017-09-01_0105Z.jpg" width="150" height="221" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e4/Sanvu_2017-09-01_0105Z.jpg/225px-Sanvu_2017-09-01_0105Z.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e4/Sanvu_2017-09-01_0105Z.jpg/300px-Sanvu_2017-09-01_0105Z.jpg 2x" data-file-width="7373" data-file-height="10857" /></a><span class="nowrap">&#160;</span><a href="/wiki/File:Sanvu_2017_track.png" class="image"><img alt="Sanvu 2017 track.png" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e2/Sanvu_2017_track.png/150px-Sanvu_2017_track.png" width="150" height="104" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e2/Sanvu_2017_track.png/225px-Sanvu_2017_track.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e2/Sanvu_2017_track.png/300px-Sanvu_2017_track.png 2x" data-file-width="2700" data-file-height="1870" /></a></span></div>\n</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<th scope="row">Duration</th>\n<td>August 26&#160;\xe2\x80\x93 September 3</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<th scope="row">Peak intensity</th>\n<td>150&#160;km/h (90&#160;mph) <small>(10-min)</small>&#160; 955&#160;<a href="/wiki/Pascal_(unit)" title="Pascal (unit)">hPa</a>&#160;(<a href="/wiki/Bar_(unit)" title="Bar (unit)">mbar</a>)</td>\n</tr>\n</table>\n<p>On August 27, the JMA began to monitor a tropical depression that had developed about 441&#160;km (274&#160;mi) north-northeast of <a href="/wiki/Saipan" title="Saipan">Saipan</a>, although the system\'s nature was more of a monsoon depression.<sup id="cite_ref-88" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-88">[87]</a></sup> The JTWC followed suit on the following day, designating the system as <i>17W</i>.<sup id="cite_ref-89" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-89">[88]</a></sup> Around the same time, the system had intensified into Tropical Storm Sanvu. By August 29, Sanvu increased in size, and therefore it prompted the JMA to upgrade it to a severe tropical storm. After moving in a westward direction, Sanvu stalled and entered a region of favorable conditions. As a ragged eye developed, both agencies upgraded Sanvu to a typhoon during August 31.<sup id="cite_ref-90" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-90">[89]</a></sup> Sanvu reached its peak intensity on September 1 as a Category 2 typhoon.<sup id="cite_ref-91" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-91">[90]</a></sup> Thereafter, the system steadily weakened as it started to move northwards with JTWC immediately downgrading the system to a tropical storm and issuing their final advisory late on September 2. The JMA still classified Sanvu as a typhoon until they issued their final advisory as the system had transitioned into an extratropical cyclone on September 3.</p>\n<p>Sanvu did not caused any significant damage in the <a href="/wiki/Mariana_Islands" title="Mariana Islands">Mariana Islands</a>, though a 33-year-old woman drowned at Obyan beach due to large waves on August 29.<sup id="cite_ref-Sanvu1_92-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Sanvu1-92">[91]</a></sup></p>\n<div style="clear:both;"></div>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Severe_Tropical_Storm_Mawar">Severe Tropical Storm Mawar</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2017_Pacific_typhoon_season&amp;action=edit&amp;section=22" title="Edit section: Severe Tropical Storm Mawar">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<table class="infobox" style="width:22em;width: 24em;">\n<tr>\n<td colspan="2" style="text-align:center;font-weight: bold; background: #ccffff">Severe tropical storm&#160;(JMA)</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td colspan="2" style="text-align:center;font-weight: bold; background: #00faf4">Tropical storm&#160;(SSHWS)</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td colspan="2" style="text-align:center">\n<div style="vertical-align: middle"><span class="nowrap"><a href="/wiki/File:Mawar_2017-09-03_0540Z.jpg" class="image"><img alt="Mawar 2017-09-03 0540Z.jpg" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/af/Mawar_2017-09-03_0540Z.jpg/150px-Mawar_2017-09-03_0540Z.jpg" width="150" height="206" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/af/Mawar_2017-09-03_0540Z.jpg/225px-Mawar_2017-09-03_0540Z.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/af/Mawar_2017-09-03_0540Z.jpg/300px-Mawar_2017-09-03_0540Z.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1995" data-file-height="2740" /></a><span class="nowrap">&#160;</span><a href="/wiki/File:Mawar_2017_track.png" class="image"><img alt="Mawar 2017 track.png" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b0/Mawar_2017_track.png/150px-Mawar_2017_track.png" width="150" height="93" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b0/Mawar_2017_track.png/225px-Mawar_2017_track.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b0/Mawar_2017_track.png/300px-Mawar_2017_track.png 2x" data-file-width="2700" data-file-height="1669" /></a></span></div>\n</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<th scope="row">Duration</th>\n<td>August 30&#160;\xe2\x80\x93 September 4</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<th scope="row">Peak intensity</th>\n<td>95&#160;km/h (60&#160;mph) <small>(10-min)</small>&#160; 990&#160;<a href="/wiki/Pascal_(unit)" title="Pascal (unit)">hPa</a>&#160;(<a href="/wiki/Bar_(unit)" title="Bar (unit)">mbar</a>)</td>\n</tr>\n</table>\n<p>On August 30, the JMA started to track a tropical depression to the north-northeast of <a href="/wiki/Luzon" title="Luzon">Luzon</a>, <a href="/wiki/Philippines" title="Philippines">Philippines</a>. Given the international designation of <i>18W</i> by the JTWC,<sup id="cite_ref-93" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-93">[92]</a></sup> the JMA upgraded the system immediately to Tropical Storm Mawar. Slowly organizing, convection had rapidly developed and Mawar strengthened into a severe tropical storm early on September 2. On September 3, Mawar had weakened to a tropical storm after environments started to become unfavorable due to high wind shear.<sup id="cite_ref-94" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-94">[93]</a></sup> Later that day, Mawar weakened to a tropical depression and the JTWC issued their final advisory while making landfall over in Southeastern China between the cities of <a href="/wiki/Shanwei" title="Shanwei">Shanwei</a> and <a href="/wiki/Shantou" title="Shantou">Shantou</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-95" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-95">[94]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Mawar1_96-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Mawar1-96">[95]</a></sup> The JMA followed suit early on September 4 when Mawar had fully dissipated.</p>\n<p>The China\'s National Meteorological Center (NMC) issued a blue alert for the southern parts of <a href="/wiki/Guangdong" title="Guangdong">Guangdong</a> on September 1.<sup id="cite_ref-97" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-97">[96]</a></sup> During 2:00&#160;a.m. local time on September 2, the <a href="/wiki/Hong_Kong_Observatory" title="Hong Kong Observatory">Hong Kong Observatory</a> issued a Tropical Cyclone Warning Signal No. 1 over in <a href="/wiki/Hong_Kong" title="Hong Kong">Hong Kong</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-98" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-98">[97]</a></sup> Chinese authorities activated a natural disaster alert and response to help local civil affairs departments in areas such as the provinces of <a href="/wiki/Fujian" title="Fujian">Fujian</a> and Guandong to prepare for relief work.<sup id="cite_ref-99" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-99">[98]</a></sup> By September 3, the NMC had raised their warning signal to a yellow alert.<sup id="cite_ref-100" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-100">[99]</a></sup> Mawar did not cause any casualties or any major damages, though flooding was a major concern with reports of rainfall of up to 80&#160;mm (3.1&#160;in) in some places which were impacted by Hato and Pakhar.<sup id="cite_ref-Mawar1_96-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Mawar1-96">[95]</a></sup></p>\n<div style="clear:both;"></div>\n<h3><span id="Tropical_Storm_Guchol_(Kiko)"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Tropical_Storm_Guchol_.28Kiko.29">Tropical Storm Guchol (Kiko)</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2017_Pacific_typhoon_season&amp;action=edit&amp;section=23" title="Edit section: Tropical Storm Guchol (Kiko)">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<table class="infobox" style="width:22em;width: 24em;">\n<tr>\n<td colspan="2" style="text-align:center;font-weight: bold; background: #00faf4">Tropical storm&#160;(JMA)</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td colspan="2" style="text-align:center;font-weight: bold; background: #5ebaff">Tropical depression&#160;(SSHWS)</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td colspan="2" style="text-align:center">\n<div style="vertical-align: middle"><span class="nowrap"><a href="/wiki/File:Guchol_2017-09-06_0305Z.jpg" class="image"><img alt="Guchol 2017-09-06 0305Z.jpg" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/bd/Guchol_2017-09-06_0305Z.jpg/150px-Guchol_2017-09-06_0305Z.jpg" width="150" height="204" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/bd/Guchol_2017-09-06_0305Z.jpg/225px-Guchol_2017-09-06_0305Z.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/bd/Guchol_2017-09-06_0305Z.jpg/300px-Guchol_2017-09-06_0305Z.jpg 2x" data-file-width="4913" data-file-height="6689" /></a><span class="nowrap">&#160;</span><a href="/wiki/File:Guchol_2017_track.png" class="image"><img alt="Guchol 2017 track.png" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d6/Guchol_2017_track.png/150px-Guchol_2017_track.png" width="150" height="93" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d6/Guchol_2017_track.png/225px-Guchol_2017_track.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d6/Guchol_2017_track.png/300px-Guchol_2017_track.png 2x" data-file-width="2700" data-file-height="1669" /></a></span></div>\n</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<th scope="row">Duration</th>\n<td>September 3&#160;\xe2\x80\x93 September 7</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<th scope="row">Peak intensity</th>\n<td>65&#160;km/h (40&#160;mph) <small>(10-min)</small>&#160; 1000&#160;<a href="/wiki/Pascal_(unit)" title="Pascal (unit)">hPa</a>&#160;(<a href="/wiki/Bar_(unit)" title="Bar (unit)">mbar</a>)</td>\n</tr>\n</table>\n<p>On September 3, the JMA started to track a tropical depression that had developed to the east of <a href="/wiki/Luzon" title="Luzon">Luzon</a>, <a href="/wiki/Philippines" title="Philippines">Philippines</a>. During the next day, the PAGASA initiated advisories and gave the local name <i>Kiko</i>,<sup id="cite_ref-101" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-101">[100]</a></sup> while the JTWC followed suit by giving it the designation <i>19W</i>.<sup id="cite_ref-102" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-102">[101]</a></sup> However, due to increased wind shear along with an exposed circulation, the JTWC issued its final advisory on 03:00 UTC September 5.<sup id="cite_ref-103" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-103">[102]</a></sup> Several hours later, deep convection was depicted and despite moderate to high shear, the JTWC re-initiated advisories,<sup id="cite_ref-104" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-104">[103]</a></sup> while the JMA had upgraded the system to a tropical storm, naming it as <i>Guchol</i> early on the next day. On 21:00 UTC of that day, the JTWC stopped issuing warnings on the system after convection significantly weakened.<sup id="cite_ref-105" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-105">[104]</a></sup> <span class="citation-needed-content" style="padding-left:0.1em; padding-right:0.1em; color:#595959; border:1px solid #DDD;">JMA later followed suit early in the next day by declaring it a remnant low as it neared <a href="/wiki/Putian" title="Putian">Putian</a>, <a href="/wiki/Fujian" title="Fujian">Fujian</a> on <a href="/wiki/Strait_of_Taiwan" class="mw-redirect" title="Strait of Taiwan">Strait of Taiwan</a>. The remnant low would then make landfall over <a href="/wiki/Pingtan_County" title="Pingtan County">Pingtan County</a> of <a href="/wiki/Fujian" title="Fujian">Fujian</a> in China late in the following day before it transitioned into an extratropical storm near <a href="/wiki/Zhejiang" title="Zhejiang">Zhejiang</a> as it merged with the cold front on September 8.</span><sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="margin-left:0.1em; white-space:nowrap;">[<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (September 2017)">citation needed</span></a></i>]</sup></p>\n<div style="clear:both;"></div>\n<h3><span id="Typhoon_Talim_(Lannie)"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Typhoon_Talim_.28Lannie.29">Typhoon Talim (Lannie)</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2017_Pacific_typhoon_season&amp;action=edit&amp;section=24" title="Edit section: Typhoon Talim (Lannie)">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<table class="infobox" style="width:22em;width: 24em;">\n<tr>\n<td colspan="2" style="text-align:center;font-weight: bold; background: #fdaf9a">Typhoon&#160;(JMA)</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td colspan="2" style="text-align:center;font-weight: bold; background: #ff8f20">Category 4&#160;typhoon&#160;(SSHWS)</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td colspan="2" style="text-align:center">\n<div style="vertical-align: middle"><span class="nowrap"><a href="/wiki/File:Talim_2017-09-14_0215Z.jpg" class="image"><img alt="Talim 2017-09-14 0215Z.jpg" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/9a/Talim_2017-09-14_0215Z.jpg/150px-Talim_2017-09-14_0215Z.jpg" width="150" height="200" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/9a/Talim_2017-09-14_0215Z.jpg/225px-Talim_2017-09-14_0215Z.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/9a/Talim_2017-09-14_0215Z.jpg/300px-Talim_2017-09-14_0215Z.jpg 2x" data-file-width="5490" data-file-height="7320" /></a><span class="nowrap">&#160;</span><a href="/wiki/File:Talim_2017_track.png" class="image"><img alt="Talim 2017 track.png" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/dd/Talim_2017_track.png/150px-Talim_2017_track.png" width="150" height="150" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/dd/Talim_2017_track.png/225px-Talim_2017_track.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/dd/Talim_2017_track.png/300px-Talim_2017_track.png 2x" data-file-width="2700" data-file-height="2700" /></a></span></div>\n</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<th scope="row">Duration</th>\n<td>September 7&#160;\xe2\x80\x93 September 18</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<th scope="row">Peak intensity</th>\n<td>175&#160;km/h (110&#160;mph) <small>(10-min)</small>&#160; 935&#160;<a href="/wiki/Pascal_(unit)" title="Pascal (unit)">hPa</a>&#160;(<a href="/wiki/Bar_(unit)" title="Bar (unit)">mbar</a>)</td>\n</tr>\n</table>\n<p>A tropical depression formed east of <a href="/wiki/Guam" title="Guam">Guam</a> on September 7.<sup id="cite_ref-106" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-106">[105]</a></sup> By the next day, the JTWC began issuing advisories on Tropical Depression 20W.<sup id="cite_ref-107" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-107">[106]</a></sup> On September 9, 20W organized into a tropical storm, with the JMA naming the system as <i>Talim</i>.<sup id="cite_ref-108" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-108">[107]</a></sup> With gradual intensification, the JMA upgraded Talim to a severe tropical storm. Talim further strengthened to a typhoon on September 11 where it simultaneously entered the PAR, with PAGASA naming it as <i>Lannie</i>.<sup id="cite_ref-109" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-109">[108]</a></sup> The JTWC, however, delayed their upgrade until September 12.<sup id="cite_ref-110" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-110">[109]</a></sup> Due to an ill-defined eye, Talim maintained its intensity until its eye became much clearer as rapid deepening ensued, as Talim became a Category 4 on September 14, and reached its peak intensity with 1-minute sustained winds of 220&#160;km/h (140&#160;mph).<sup id="cite_ref-111" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-111">[110]</a></sup> Talim began to curve eastward as it rapidly weakened to a tropical storm thereafter, making landfall in <a href="/wiki/Kyushu" title="Kyushu">Kyushu</a> on September 17, with a path of heavy rainfall up to the region east of Tokyo.<sup id="cite_ref-112" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-112">[111]</a></sup></p>\n<p>As of September 18, the death toll from Talim stands at two while 38 are injured.<sup id="cite_ref-Talim1_113-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Talim1-113">[112]</a></sup>Total economic losses in Hokkaido were counted to be 6.3 billion JPY(USD 55.7 miilion).<sup id="cite_ref-Talim2_114-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Talim2-114">[113]</a></sup> Total Aquaculture losses in Mainland Japan were counted to be JPY 100 million(USD 0.88 million).<sup id="cite_ref-Talim3_115-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Talim3-115">[114]</a></sup> Total agriculture losses in Mainland Japan were counted to be JPY 19.2 billion(USD 168.71 million).<sup id="cite_ref-Talim4_116-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Talim4-116">[115]</a></sup></p>\n<div style="clear:both;"></div>\n<h3><span id="Typhoon_Doksuri_(Maring)"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Typhoon_Doksuri_.28Maring.29">Typhoon Doksuri (Maring)</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2017_Pacific_typhoon_season&amp;action=edit&amp;section=25" title="Edit section: Typhoon Doksuri (Maring)">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<table class="infobox" style="width:22em;width: 24em;">\n<tr>\n<td colspan="2" style="text-align:center;font-weight: bold; background: #fdaf9a">Typhoon&#160;(JMA)</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td colspan="2" style="text-align:center;font-weight: bold; background: #ffc140">Category 3&#160;typhoon&#160;(SSHWS)</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td colspan="2" style="text-align:center">\n<div style="vertical-align: middle"><span class="nowrap"><a href="/wiki/File:Doksuri_2017-09-14_0548Z.jpg" class="image"><img alt="Doksuri 2017-09-14 0548Z.jpg" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/84/Doksuri_2017-09-14_0548Z.jpg/150px-Doksuri_2017-09-14_0548Z.jpg" width="150" height="194" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/84/Doksuri_2017-09-14_0548Z.jpg/225px-Doksuri_2017-09-14_0548Z.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/84/Doksuri_2017-09-14_0548Z.jpg/300px-Doksuri_2017-09-14_0548Z.jpg 2x" data-file-width="4536" data-file-height="5872" /></a><span class="nowrap">&#160;</span><a href="/wiki/File:Doksuri_2017_track.png" class="image"><img alt="Doksuri 2017 track.png" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d4/Doksuri_2017_track.png/150px-Doksuri_2017_track.png" width="150" height="93" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d4/Doksuri_2017_track.png/225px-Doksuri_2017_track.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d4/Doksuri_2017_track.png/300px-Doksuri_2017_track.png 2x" data-file-width="2700" data-file-height="1669" /></a></span></div>\n</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<th scope="row">Duration</th>\n<td>September 10&#160;\xe2\x80\x93 September 16</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<th scope="row">Peak intensity</th>\n<td>150&#160;km/h (90&#160;mph) <small>(10-min)</small>&#160; 955&#160;<a href="/wiki/Pascal_(unit)" title="Pascal (unit)">hPa</a>&#160;(<a href="/wiki/Bar_(unit)" title="Bar (unit)">mbar</a>)</td>\n</tr>\n</table>\n<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Typhoon_Doksuri_(2017)" title="Typhoon Doksuri (2017)">Typhoon Doksuri (2017)</a></div>\n<p>As of September 19, the NDRRMC confirmed a total of 8 dead due to landslides and flooding while total damages were up to Ph\xe2\x82\xb1267 million (US$5.23 million).<sup id="cite_ref-Doksuri1_117-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Doksuri1-117">[116]</a></sup></p>\n<p>On September 15, Typhoon Doksuri made landfall in Qu\xe1\xba\xa3ng B\xc3\xacnh Province, Vietnam as a Category 3 typhoon. Doksuri killed 15 people so far in Vietnam while estimated damages were about \xe2\x82\xab16.36 trillion (US$720 million).<sup id="cite_ref-Doksuri2_118-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Doksuri2-118">[117]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Doksuri3_119-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Doksuri3-119">[118]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Doksuri5_120-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Doksuri5-120">[119]</a></sup> Despite making landfall in Indochina, Doksuri affected Hainan and total economic losses were estimated to be CNY 59 million(USD 8.96 million).<sup id="cite_ref-Doksuri4_121-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Doksuri4-121">[120]</a></sup></p>\n<div style="clear:both;"></div>\n<h3><span id="Tropical_Depression_22W_(Nando)"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Tropical_Depression_22W_.28Nando.29">Tropical Depression 22W (Nando)</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2017_Pacific_typhoon_season&amp;action=edit&amp;section=26" title="Edit section: Tropical Depression 22W (Nando)">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<table class="infobox" style="width:22em;width: 24em;">\n<tr>\n<td colspan="2" style="text-align:center;font-weight: bold; background: #5ebaff">Tropical depression&#160;(JMA)</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td colspan="2" style="text-align:center;font-weight: bold; background: #5ebaff">Tropical depression&#160;(SSHWS)</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td colspan="2" style="text-align:center">\n<div style="vertical-align: middle"><span class="nowrap"><a href="/wiki/File:Nando_2017-09-25_0335Z.jpg" class="image"><img alt="Nando 2017-09-25 0335Z.jpg" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/7e/Nando_2017-09-25_0335Z.jpg/150px-Nando_2017-09-25_0335Z.jpg" width="150" height="208" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/7e/Nando_2017-09-25_0335Z.jpg/225px-Nando_2017-09-25_0335Z.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/7e/Nando_2017-09-25_0335Z.jpg/300px-Nando_2017-09-25_0335Z.jpg 2x" data-file-width="5793" data-file-height="8017" /></a><span class="nowrap">&#160;</span><a href="/wiki/File:Nando_2017_track.png" class="image"><img alt="Nando 2017 track.png" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/7a/Nando_2017_track.png/150px-Nando_2017_track.png" width="150" height="93" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/7a/Nando_2017_track.png/225px-Nando_2017_track.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/7a/Nando_2017_track.png/300px-Nando_2017_track.png 2x" data-file-width="2700" data-file-height="1669" /></a></span></div>\n</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<th scope="row">Duration</th>\n<td>September 23&#160;\xe2\x80\x93 September 25</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<th scope="row">Peak intensity</th>\n<td>55&#160;km/h (35&#160;mph) <small>(10-min)</small>&#160; 1002&#160;<a href="/wiki/Pascal_(unit)" title="Pascal (unit)">hPa</a>&#160;(<a href="/wiki/Bar_(unit)" title="Bar (unit)">mbar</a>)</td>\n</tr>\n</table>\n<p>A tropical depression formed to the west of Luzon on September 23, and was named "Nando" by PAGASA. The tropical depression quickly moved west-northwest and made landfall in Qu\xe1\xba\xa3ng Ninh, Vietnam, on September 25, before dissipating later on the same day.</p>\n<p>The China Observatory issued a "yellow" alert over in the eastern and southern regions due to rainstorms. Some areas have warned a possible precipitation of about 140&#160;mm (5.5&#160;in).<sup id="cite_ref-122" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-122">[121]</a></sup> Typhoon Signal No. 1 was raised over in <a href="/wiki/Hong_Kong" title="Hong Kong">Hong Kong</a> during September 24, with expected gusts of up to 70&#160;km/h (42&#160;mph) including rough swells.<sup id="cite_ref-123" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-123">[122]</a></sup> A voltage dip also occurred, causing 17 people to be trapped in lifts.<sup id="cite_ref-124" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-124">[123]</a></sup> As the depression approached <a href="/wiki/Vietnam" title="Vietnam">Vietnam</a> on September 25, the Vietnam National Center for Hydro-Meteorological Forecasting of Vietnam forecast rainfall of about 150&#160;mm (5.9&#160;in) in <a href="/wiki/Hanoi" title="Hanoi">Hanoi</a> and surrounding provinces, with rough waves up to 3&#160;m (9.8&#160;ft) in <a href="/wiki/Ha_Long_Bay" class="mw-redirect" title="Ha Long Bay">Ha Long Bay</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-125" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-125">[124]</a></sup></p>\n<div style="clear:both;"></div>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Tropical_Depression_23W">Tropical Depression 23W</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2017_Pacific_typhoon_season&amp;action=edit&amp;section=27" title="Edit section: Tropical Depression 23W">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<table class="infobox" style="width:22em;width: 24em;">\n<tr>\n<td colspan="2" style="text-align:center;font-weight: bold; background: #5ebaff">Tropical depression&#160;(JMA)</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td colspan="2" style="text-align:center;font-weight: bold; background: #5ebaff">Tropical depression&#160;(SSHWS)</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td colspan="2" style="text-align:center">\n<div style="vertical-align: middle"><span class="nowrap"><a href="/wiki/File:23W_2017-10-08_0610Z.jpg" class="image"><img alt="23W 2017-10-08 0610Z.jpg" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/31/23W_2017-10-08_0610Z.jpg/150px-23W_2017-10-08_0610Z.jpg" width="150" height="217" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/31/23W_2017-10-08_0610Z.jpg/225px-23W_2017-10-08_0610Z.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/31/23W_2017-10-08_0610Z.jpg/300px-23W_2017-10-08_0610Z.jpg 2x" data-file-width="2416" data-file-height="3501" /></a><span class="nowrap">&#160;</span><a href="/wiki/File:23W_2017_track.png" class="image"><img alt="23W 2017 track.png" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/85/23W_2017_track.png/150px-23W_2017_track.png" width="150" height="93" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/85/23W_2017_track.png/225px-23W_2017_track.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/85/23W_2017_track.png/300px-23W_2017_track.png 2x" data-file-width="2700" data-file-height="1669" /></a></span></div>\n</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<th scope="row">Duration</th>\n<td>October 7&#160;\xe2\x80\x93 October 10</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<th scope="row">Peak intensity</th>\n<td>55&#160;km/h (35&#160;mph) <small>(10-min)</small>&#160; 1000&#160;<a href="/wiki/Pascal_(unit)" title="Pascal (unit)">hPa</a>&#160;(<a href="/wiki/Bar_(unit)" title="Bar (unit)">mbar</a>)</td>\n</tr>\n</table>\n<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Tropical_Depression_23W" title="Tropical Depression 23W">Tropical Depression 23W</a></div>\n<p>Early on October 7, a tropical depression formed to the west of the Philippines.<sup id="cite_ref-126" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-126">[125]</a></sup></p>\n<p>Early on October 10, the tropical depression made landfall in H\xc3\xa0 T\xc4\xa9nh Province, Vietnam, and dissipated shortly afterward. Consequently, both the JMA and the JTWC issued their final advisories for the storm.</p>\n<p>Tropical Depression 23W caused severe flooding over provinces of Northern and Central Vietnam. Roughly more than 700 houses have been destroyed, while rescue efforts have saved 28 people from the danger zone. So far at least 83 people were killed, and damages were about 9.27 trillion\xe2\x82\xab (US$409 million).<sup id="cite_ref-23W1_127-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-23W1-127">[126]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-23W2_128-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-23W2-128">[127]</a></sup> During October 10, the <a href="/wiki/Red_River_(Asia)" title="Red River (Asia)">Red River</a> was forecast to have waters exceed to the levels of 3\xe2\x80\x9350&#160;cm (2\xe2\x80\x9320&#160;in).<sup id="cite_ref-129" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-129">[128]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-130" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-130">[129]</a></sup> In Ho\xc3\xa0ng Long river (Ninh B\xc3\xacnh Province) flooding was the most severe since 1985.<sup id="cite_ref-131" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-131">[130]</a></sup></p>\n<div style="clear:both;"></div>\n<h3><span id="Typhoon_Khanun_(Odette)"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Typhoon_Khanun_.28Odette.29">Typhoon Khanun (Odette)</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2017_Pacific_typhoon_season&amp;action=edit&amp;section=28" title="Edit section: Typhoon Khanun (Odette)">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<table class="infobox" style="width:22em;width: 24em;">\n<tr>\n<td colspan="2" style="text-align:center;font-weight: bold; background: href="/wiki/Pascal_(unit)" title="Pascal (unit)">hPa</a>&#160;(<a href="/wiki/Bar_(unit)" title="Bar (unit)">mbar</a>)</td>\n</tr>\n</table>\n<table class="plainlinks metadata ambox mbox-small-left ambox-content" role="presentation">\n<tr>\n<td class="mbox-image"><a href="/wiki/File:Wiki_letter_w_cropped.svg" class="image"><img alt="[icon]" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1c/Wiki_letter_w_cropped.svg/20px-Wiki_letter_w_cropped.svg.png" width="20" height="14" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1c/Wiki_letter_w_cropped.svg/30px-Wiki_letter_w_cropped.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1c/Wiki_letter_w_cropped.svg/40px-Wiki_letter_w_cropped.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="44" data-file-height="31" /></a></td>\n<td class="mbox-text">\n<div class="mbox-text-span"><b>This section needs expansion</b>. <small>You can help by <a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=2017_Pacific_typhoon_season&amp;action=edit&amp;section=">adding to it</a>.</small> <small><i>(October 2017)</i></small></div>\n</td>\n</tr>\n</table>\n<p>According to the NDRRMC, Khanun killed only one person, with total damages of Php4.45 million (US$86,400).<sup id="cite_ref-Khanun4_132-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Khanun4-132">[131]</a></sup> Total economic damages in Mainland China amounted to CNY 1.35 billion (USD 203.8 million), including 430 million CNY in Zhejiang province, 848 million CNY in Guangdong Province, 70 million in Hainan.<sup id="cite_ref-Khanun1_133-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Khanun1-133">[132]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Khanun2_134-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Khanun2-134">[133]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Khanun3_135-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Khanun3-135">[134]</a></sup> Authorities in Hong Kong and Macau raised the number 8 tropical cyclone warning on October 15 as gale force winds affected the region.</p>\n<div style="clear:both;"></div>\n<h3><span id="Typhoon_Lan_(Paolo)"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Typhoon_Lan_.28Paolo.29">Typhoon Lan (Paolo)</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2017_Pacific_typhoon_season&amp;action=edit&amp;section=29" title="Edit section: Typhoon Lan (Paolo)">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<table class="infobox" style="width:22em;width: 24em;">\n<tr>\n<td colspan="2" style="text-align:center;font-weight: bold; background: #fdaf9a">Typhoon&#160;(JMA)</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td colspan="2" style="text-align:center;font-weight: bold; background: #ff8f20">Category 4&#160;super&#160;typhoon&#160;(SSHWS)</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td colspan="2" style="text-align:center">\n<div style="vertical-align: middle"><span class="nowrap"><a href="/wiki/File:Lan_2017-10-21_0412Z.jpg" class="image"><img alt="Lan 2017-10-21 0412Z.jpg" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/2c/Lan_2017-10-21_0412Z.jpg/150px-Lan_2017-10-21_0412Z.jpg" width="150" height="200" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/2c/Lan_2017-10-21_0412Z.jpg/225px-Lan_2017-10-21_0412Z.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/2c/Lan_2017-10-21_0412Z.jpg/300px-Lan_2017-10-21_0412Z.jpg 2x" data-file-width="3600" data-file-height="4800" /></a><span class="nowrap">&#160;</span><a href="/wiki/File:Lan_2017_track.png" class="image"><img alt="Lan 2017 track.png" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a4/Lan_2017_track.png/150px-Lan_2017_track.png" width="150" height="150" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a4/Lan_2017_track.png/225px-Lan_2017_track.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a4/Lan_2017_track.png/300px-Lan_2017_track.png 2x" data-file-width="2700" data-file-height="2700" /></a></span></div>\n</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<th scope="row">Duration</th>\n<td>October 14&#160;\xe2\x80\x93 October 23</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<th scope="row">Peak intensity</th>\n<td>175&#160;km/h (110&#160;mph) <small>(10-min)</small>&#160; 925&#160;<a href="/wiki/Pascal_(unit)" title="Pascal (unit)">hPa</a>&#160;(<a href="/wiki/Bar_(unit)" title="Bar (unit)">mbar</a>)</td>\n</tr>\n</table>\n<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Typhoon_Lan_(2017)" title="Typhoon Lan (2017)">Typhoon Lan (2017)</a></div>\n<p>The <a href="/wiki/United_States_Naval_Research_Laboratory" title="United States Naval Research Laboratory">United States Naval Research Laboratory</a> (NRL) initially mentioned a tropical disturbance over <a href="/wiki/Chuuk_State" title="Chuuk State">Chuuk</a> on October 11.<sup id="cite_ref-136" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-136">[135]</a></sup> After the slow consolidation, the <a href="/wiki/Joint_Typhoon_Warning_Center" title="Joint Typhoon Warning Center">Joint Typhoon Warning Center</a> (JTWC) issued a <a href="/wiki/Tropical_Cyclone_Formation_Alert" title="Tropical Cyclone Formation Alert">Tropical Cyclone Formation Alert</a> to the elongated system early on October 14,<sup id="cite_ref-137" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-137">[136]</a></sup> shortly after the <a href="/wiki/Japan_Meteorological_Agency" title="Japan Meteorological Agency">Japan Meteorological Agency</a> (JMA) started to monitor it as a <a href="/wiki/Low-pressure_area" title="Low-pressure area">low-pressure area</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-138" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-138">[137]</a></sup> The agency upgraded it to a tropical depression almost one day later and began to issue tropical cyclone warnings since 06:00 <a href="/wiki/Coordinated_Universal_Time" title="Coordinated Universal Time">UTC</a> on October 15.<sup id="cite_ref-139" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-139">[138]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-140" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-140">[139]</a></sup> In the afternoon, the JTWC also upgraded it to a tropical depression assigning the designation <i>25W</i>, which formative but shallow convective <a href="/wiki/Rainband" title="Rainband">bands</a> had become more organized, and symmetrically wrapped into a defined low-level circulation center.<sup id="cite_ref-141" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-141">[140]</a></sup> About three hours later, the JMA upgraded it to the twenty-first Northwest Pacific tropical storm in 2017 and assigned the international name <i>Lan</i>, when it was located approximately 310&#160;km (190&#160;mi) to the northeast of <a href="/wiki/Palau" title="Palau">Palau</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-142" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-142">[141]</a></sup> Early on October 16, the JTWC upgraded Lan to a tropical storm too, based on T-number 2.5 of the <a href="/wiki/Dvorak_technique" title="Dvorak technique">Dvorak technique</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-143" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-143">[142]</a></sup> shortly before it entered the Philippine Area of Responsibility and received the name <i>Paolo</i> from <a href="/wiki/PAGASA" title="PAGASA">PAGASA</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-144" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-144">[143]</a></sup></p>\n<div style="clear:both;"></div>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Tropical_Depression_26W">Tropical Depression 26W</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2017_Pacific_typhoon_season&amp;action=edit&amp;section=30" title="Edit section: Tropical Depression 26W">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<table class="infobox" style="width:22em;width: 24em;">\n<tr>\n<td colspan="2" style="text-align:center;font-weight: bold; background: #5ebaff">Tropical depression&#160;(SSHWS)</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td colspan="2" style="text-align:center">\n<div style="vertical-align: middle"><span class="nowrap"><a href="/wiki/File:26W_2017-10-19_0550Z.jpg" class="image"><img alt="26W 2017-10-19 0550Z.jpg" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/48/26W_2017-10-19_0550Z.jpg/150px-26W_2017-10-19_0550Z.jpg" width="150" height="195" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/48/26W_2017-10-19_0550Z.jpg/225px-26W_2017-10-19_0550Z.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/48/26W_2017-10-19_0550Z.jpg/300px-26W_2017-10-19_0550Z.jpg 2x" data-file-width="5281" data-file-height="6881" /></a><span class="nowrap">&#160;</span><a href="/wiki/File:26W_2017_track.png" class="image"><img alt="26W 2017 track.png" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/08/26W_2017_track.png/150px-26W_2017_track.png" width="150" height="93" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/08/26W_2017_track.png/225px-26W_2017_track.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/08/26W_2017_track.png/300px-26W_2017_track.png 2x" data-file-width="2700" data-file-height="1669" /></a></span></div>\n</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<th scope="row">Duration</th>\n<td>October 18&#160;\xe2\x80\x93 October 19</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<th scope="row">Peak intensity</th>\n<td>45&#160;km/h (30&#160;mph)&#160;<small>(1-min)</small>&#160; 1002&#160;<a href="/wiki/Pascal_(unit)" title="Pascal (unit)">hPa</a>&#160;(<a href="/wiki/Bar_(unit)" title="Bar (unit)">mbar</a>)</td>\n</tr>\n</table>\n<p>Formed from an enhanced <a href="/wiki/Southwest_monsoon" class="mw-redirect" title="Southwest monsoon">monsoon</a>, a tropical disturbance had developed just to the northwest of <a href="/wiki/Palawan" title="Palawan">Palawan</a> on October 17.<sup id="cite_ref-145" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-145">[144]</a></sup> On October 18, the JTWC had issued a TCFA on the system.<sup id="cite_ref-146" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-146">[145]</a></sup> By 21:00 UTC of that day, the JTWC began issuing advisories as they classified it as a tropical depression, assigning the identifier <i>26W</i>.<sup id="cite_ref-147" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-147">[146]</a></sup> This was due to deep convection found near the storm\'s center with formative banding, along with its location over in a favorable environment.<sup id="cite_ref-148" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-148">[147]</a></sup> Initially, its forecast stated that 26W would intensify into a weak tropical storm, although due to a disorganized center with strong shear, the JTWC issued their final advisory on October 19 as it was being absorbed by the outflow of nearby <a href="/wiki/Typhoon_Lan" class="mw-redirect" title="Typhoon Lan">Typhoon Lan</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-149" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-149">[148]</a></sup></p>\n<p>Associated with the rainbands of a nearby typhoon, 26W helped spread scattered rainfall throughout most of <a href="/wiki/Visayas" title="Visayas">Visayas</a> and northern <a href="/wiki/Mindanao" title="Mindanao">Mindanao</a>. Residents in some areas were alerted against possible flash floods and landslides.<sup id="cite_ref-150" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-150">[149]</a></sup> 14 people were dead from heavy rainfall from the system and its precursor, and raised a <a href="/wiki/State_of_calamity" class="mw-redirect" title="State of calamity">state of calamity</a> in <a href="/wiki/Zamboanga_City" title="Zamboanga City">Zamboanga City</a> on October 23.<sup id="cite_ref-151" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-151">[150]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-26W1_152-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-26W1-152">[151]</a></sup></p>\n<div style="clear:both;"></div>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Tropical_Storm_Saola">Tropical Storm Saola</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2017_Pacific_typhoon_season&amp;action=edit&amp;section=31" title="Edit section: Tropical Storm Saola">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<table class="infobox" style="width:22em;border-collapse:collapse; width:280px">\n<tr>\n<th colspan="2" style="text-align:center;font-size:125%;font-weight:bold;font-size:12pt; background-color:#EEE; padding:0; border-bottom:#aaa 1px solid;">\n<table style="width:100%; margin:0; border-collapse:collapse;">\n<tr>\n<td style="padding:0.3em; text-align:center;border-right:1px #aaa solid;">Saola</td>\n<td style="width:24px; text-align:center; border-left:1px #aaa solid; padding:0.3em; background: #00faf4;">TS</td>\n</tr>\n</table>\n</th>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td colspan="2" style="text-align:center;border-top:#aaa 1px solid; border-bottom:#aaa 1px solid;">\n<div style="width:100%; height:100%;background: #00faf4;"><b>Current storm status</b><br />\n<b><a href="/wiki/Tropical_cyclone#Intensity_classifications" title="Tropical cyclone">Tropical storm</a></b> &#160;(<a href="/wiki/Japan_Meteorological_Agency" title="Japan Meteorological Agency">JMA</a>)</div>\n</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td colspan="2" style="text-align:center;border-top:#aaa 1px solid; border-bottom:#aaa 1px solid;">\n<div style="width:100%; height:100%;background: #00faf4;"><b>Current storm status</b><br />\n<b><a href="/wiki/Tropical_cyclone#Intensity_classifications" title="Tropical cyclone">Tropical storm</a></b>&#160;(<a href="/wiki/Saffir%E2%80%93Simpson_hurricane_wind_scale" class="mw-redirect" title="Saffir\xe2\x80\x93Simpson hurricane wind scale">1-min mean</a>)</div>\n</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td colspan="2" style="text-align:center">\n<table style="width:100%; border-collapse:collapse; font-size:94%; line-height:125%;">\n<tr style="vertical-align:top">\n<td style="text-align:center;"><a href="/wiki/File:Saola_Geostationary_VIS-IR_2017.png" class="image"><img alt="Saola Geostationary VIS-IR 2017.png" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/39/Saola_Geostationary_VIS-IR_2017.png/130px-Saola_Geostationary_VIS-IR_2017.png" width="130" height="130" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/39/Saola_Geostationary_VIS-IR_2017.png/195px-Saola_Geostationary_VIS-IR_2017.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/39/Saola_Geostationary_VIS-IR_2017.png/260px-Saola_Geostationary_VIS-IR_2017.png 2x" data-file-width="1280" data-file-height="1280" /></a>\n<div style="font-size:85%">Satellite image</div>\n</td>\n<td style="text-align:center;"><a href="/wiki/File:JTWC_wp2717.gif" class="image"><img alt="JTWC wp2717.gif" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/JTWC_wp2717.gif/170px-JTWC_wp2717.gif" width="170" height="97" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/JTWC_wp2717.gif/255px-JTWC_wp2717.gif 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/JTWC_wp2717.gif/340px-JTWC_wp2717.gif 2x" data-file-width="1665" data-file-height="950" /></a>\n<div style="font-size:85%">Forecast map</div>\n</td>\n</tr>\n</table>\n</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<th scope="row" style="padding-left:0.3em; border-top: #aaa 1px solid;">As of:</th>\n<td style="width:80%; border-top: #aaa 1px solid;">21:00 <a href="/wiki/UTC" class="mw-redirect" title="UTC">UTC</a>, October 24</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<th scope="row" style="padding-left:0.3em; border-top: #aaa 1px solid;">Location:</th>\n<td style="width:80%; border-top: #aaa 1px solid;"><span class="plainlinks nourlexpansion"><a class="external text" href="//tools.wmflabs.org/geohack/geohack.php?pagename=2017_Pacific_typhoon_season&amp;params=13.3_N_135.1_E_dim:1000km&amp;title=Saola"><span class="geo-nondefault"><span class="geo-dms" title="Maps, aerial photos, and other data for this location"><span class="latitude">13\xc2\xb018\xe2\x80\xb2N</span> <span class="longitude">135\xc2\xb006\xe2\x80\xb2E</span></span></span><span class="geo-multi-punct">\xef\xbb\xbf / \xef\xbb\xbf</span><span class="geo-default"><span class="vcard"><span class="geo-dec" title="Maps, aerial photos, and other data for this location">13.3\xc2\xb0N 135.1\xc2\xb0E</span><span style="display:none">\xef\xbb\xbf / <span class="geo">13.3; 135.1</span></span><span style="display:none">\xef\xbb\xbf (<span class="fn org">Saola</span>)</span></span></span></a></span><br />\n256&#160;nmi (474&#160;km; 295&#160;mi) <a href="/wiki/Points_of_the_compass" title="Points of the compass">NNW</a> of <a href="/wiki/Yap" title="Yap">Yap</a></td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<th scope="row" style="padding-left:0.3em; border-top: #aaa 1px solid;">Sustained winds:</th>\n<td style="width:80%; border-top: #aaa 1px solid;">75 km/h (45 mph) <small>(10-min mean)</small><br />\n65 <a href="/wiki/Km/h" class="mw-redirect" title="Km/h">km/h</a> (40 <a href="/wiki/Mph" class="mw-redirect mw-disambig" title="Mph">mph</a>) <small>(1-min mean)</small><br />\ngusting to 110 km/h (70 mph)</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<th scope="row" style="padding-left:0.3em; border-top: #aaa 1px solid;">Pressure:</th>\n<td style="width:80%; border-top: #aaa 1px solid;">998 <a href="/wiki/HPa" class="mw-redirect" title="HPa">hPa</a> (29.47 <a href="/wiki/InHg" class="mw-redirect" title="InHg">inHg</a>)</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<th scope="row" style="padding-left:0.3em; border-top: #aaa 1px solid;">Movement:</th>\n<td style="width:80%; border-top: #aaa 1px solid;"><a href="/wiki/Points_of_the_compass" title="Points of the compass">WNW</a> at 20&#160;kn (37&#160;km/h; 23&#160;mph)</td>\n</tr>\n<tr>\n<td colspan="2" style="text-align:center;border-top:#aaa 1px solid; background: #00faf4;">\n<dl>\n<dt><b>See more <a href="#Current_storm_information">detailed information</a>.</b></dt>\n</dl>\n</td>\n</tr>\n</table>\n<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Current_storm_information">Current storm information</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2017_Pacific_typhoon_season&amp;action=edit&amp;section=32" title="Edit section: Current storm information">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>\n<p>As of 21:00&#160;<a href="/wiki/Coordinated_Universal_Time" title="Coordinated Universal Time">UTC</a> October&#160;24, Tropical Storm Saola was located about <span class="plainlinks nourlexpansion"><a class="external text" href="//tools.wmflabs.org/geohack/geohack.php?pagename=2017_Pacific_typhoon_season&amp;params=13.3_N_135.1_E_dim:110km&amp;title=Saola"><span class="geo-nondefault"><span class="geo-dms" title="Maps, aerial photos, and other data for this location"><span class="latitude">13\xc2\xb018\xe2\x80\xb2N</span> <span class="longitude">135\xc2\xb006\xe2\x80\xb2E</span></span></span><span class="geo-multi-punct">\xef\xbb\xbf / \xef\xbb\xbf</span><span class="geo-default"><span class="vcard"><span class="geo-dec" title="Maps, aerial photos, and other data for this location">13.3\xc2\xb0N 135.1\xc2\xb0E</span><span style="display:none">\xef\xbb\xbf / <span class="geo">13.3; 135.1</span></span><span style="display:none">\xef\xbb\xbf (<span class="fn org">Saola</span>)</span></span></span></a></span>, about 256 nautical miles (474 kilometres; 295 miles) north-northwest of <a href="/wiki/Yap" title="Yap">Yap</a>. 10-minute sustained winds are at 40&#160;knots (75&#160;km/h; 45&#160;mph); 1-minute sustained winds are at 35&#160;knots (65&#160;km/h; 40&#160;mph), with gusts up to 60&#160;knots (110&#160;km/h; 70&#160;mph). The minimum barometric pressure is at 998&#160;<a href="/wiki/Pascal_(unit)" title="Pascal (unit)">hPa</a> (29.47&#160;<a href="/wiki/Inch_of_mercury" title="Inch of mercury">inHg</a>), and the system is moving west-northwest at 20&#160;kn (37&#160;km/h; 23&#160;mph).</p>\n<p>For latest official information, see:</p>\n<ul>\n<li>The JMA\'s <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.jma.go.jp/en/typh/1722.html">latest public advisory on Tropical Storm 1722 (Saola)</a></li>\n<li>The JTWC\'s <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://metoc.ndbc.noaa.gov/ProductFeeds-portlet/img/jtwc/products/wp2717web.txt">latest public advisory on Tropical Storm 27W (Saola)</a></li>\n</ul>\n<div style="clear:both;"></div>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Other_systems">Other systems</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2017_Pacific_typhoon_season&amp;action=edit&amp;section=33" title="Edit section: Other systems">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<p>On March 19, a tropical depression formed close to the northeast of <a href="/wiki/Mindanao" title="Mindanao">Mindanao</a>, <a href="/wiki/Philippines" title="Philippines">Philippines</a>, and dissipated over the <a href="/wiki/Sibuyan_Sea" title="Sibuyan Sea">Sibuyan Sea</a> two days later.<sup id="cite_ref-153" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-153">[152]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-154" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-154">[153]</a></sup> Early on June 29, the JMA initiated advisories on a newly formed tropical depression located about 138&#160;km (86&#160;mi) south of <a href="/wiki/Okinawa_Island" title="Okinawa Island">Okinawa Island</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-155" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-155">[154]</a></sup> The system re-curved and started moving in a northeastward direction until it dissipated to the southwest of <a href="/wiki/Tokyo" title="Tokyo">Tokyo</a> on July 1.<sup id="cite_ref-156" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-156">[155]</a></sup> Early on July 4, the JMA indicated that a tropical depression had formed about 505&#160;km (314&#160;mi) south of <a href="/wiki/Okinotorishima" title="Okinotorishima">Okinotorishima</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-157" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-157">[156]</a></sup> During the next day, the JTWC issued a <a href="/wiki/Tropical_Cyclone_Formation_Alert" title="Tropical Cyclone Formation Alert">Tropical Cyclone Formation Alert</a> (TCFA) on the system, although it was canceled several hours later.<sup id="cite_ref-158" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-158">[157]</a></sup> After moving northward, the depression rapidly weakened as it was absorbed by a <a href="/wiki/Stationary_front" title="Stationary front">stationary front</a> on July 7.<sup id="cite_ref-159" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-159">[158]</a></sup></p>\n<p>Early on July 13, the JMA reported that a non-tropical low had transitioned into a tropical depression about 72&#160;km (45&#160;mi) north-northeast of <a href="/wiki/Iwo_Jima" title="Iwo Jima">Iwo Jima</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-160" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-160">[159]</a></sup> The depression moved in a generally northeasterly direction until weakening to a low-pressure area by 06:00 UTC on July 16.<sup id="cite_ref-161" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-161">[160]</a></sup> A tropical depression formed about 691&#160;km (429&#160;mi) northeast of <a href="/wiki/Wake_Island" title="Wake Island">Wake Island</a> late on July 25, though the JTWC indicated it as a subtropical system with estimated recorded winds of 65&#160;km/h (40&#160;mph).<sup id="cite_ref-162" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-162">[161]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-163" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-163">[162]</a></sup> After several days, the system had already transitioned into an extratropical cyclone on July 29, without becoming a tropical storm.<sup id="cite_ref-164" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-164">[163]</a></sup> Early on August 25 the JMA started to track a tropical depression over in the <a href="/wiki/South_China_Sea" title="South China Sea">South China Sea</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-165" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-165">[164]</a></sup> although it was last monitored during the next day when it got absorbed by the outflow of <a href="/wiki/Tropical_Storm_Pakhar_(2017)" title="Tropical Storm Pakhar (2017)">Tropical Storm Pakhar</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-166" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-166">[165]</a></sup> On August 28, the JMA started to issue advisories on a tropical depression that had developed about 1,217&#160;km (756&#160;mi) east-northeast of <a href="/wiki/Tuguegarao_City" class="mw-redirect" title="Tuguegarao City">Tuguegarao City</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-167" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-167">[166]</a></sup> The JMA predicted that the system would become a tropical storm within the next 24 hours, although because the system did not develop further, the JMA issued their final advisory on 03:00 UTC of August 29 when the system had weakened into a low-pressure area.<sup id="cite_ref-168" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-168">[167]</a></sup> The remnants of the system helped with formation of Tropical Storm Mawar.<sup id="cite_ref-169" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-169">[168]</a></sup></p>\n<div style="clear:both;"></div>\n<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Storm_names">Storm names</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2017_Pacific_typhoon_season&amp;action=edit&amp;section=34" title="Edit section: Storm names">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>\n<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">See also: <a href="/wiki/Tropical_cyclone_naming" title="Tropical cyclone naming">Tropical cyclone naming</a> and <a href="/wiki/History_of_tropical_cyclone_naming" title="History of tropical cyclone naming">History of tropical cyclone naming</a></div>\n<p>Within the Northwest Pacific Ocean, both the <a href="/wiki/Japan_Meteorological_Agency" title="Japan Meteorological Agency">Japan Meteorological Agency</a> (JMA) and PAGASA assign names to tropical cyclones that develop in the Western Pacific, which can result in a tropical cyclone having two names.<sup id="cite_ref-Padgett_Dec_99_170-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Padgett_Dec_99-170">[169]</a></sup> The Japan Meteorological Agency\'s RSMC Tokyo&#160;\xe2\x80\x94 Typhoon Center assigns international names to tropical cyclones on behalf of the <a href="/wiki/World_Meteorological_Organization" title="World Meteorological Organization">World Meteorological Organization</a>\'s Typhoon Committee, should they be judged to have 10-minute sustained windspeeds of 65&#160;km/h (40&#160;mph).<sup id="cite_ref-TC_171-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-TC-171">[170]</a></sup> PAGASA assigns names to tropical cyclones which move into or form as a tropical depression in their area of responsibility located between 135\xc2\xb0E\xe2\x80\x93115\xc2\xb0E and between 5\xc2\xb0N\xe2\x80\x9325\xc2\xb0N even if the cyclone has had an international name assigned to it.<sup id="cite_ref-Padgett_Dec_99_170-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Padgett_Dec_99-170">[169]</a></sup> The names of significant tropical cyclones are retired, by both <a href="/wiki/List_of_retired_Philippine_typhoon_names" title="List of retired Philippine typhoon names">PAGASA</a> and the <a href="/wiki/List_of_retired_Pacific_typhoon_names_(JMA)" class="mw-redirect" title="List of retired Pacific typhoon names (JMA)">Typhoon Committee</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-TC_171-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-TC-171">[170]</a></sup> Should the list of names for the Philippine region be exhausted then names will be taken from an auxiliary list of which the first ten are published each season. Unused names are marked in <span style="color:#666666">gray</span>.</p>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="International_names">International names</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2017_Pacific_typhoon_season&amp;action=edit&amp;section=35" title="Edit section: International names">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">Main article: <a href="/wiki/List_of_retired_Pacific_typhoon_names" title="List of retired Pacific typhoon names">List of retired Pacific typhoon names</a></div>\n<p>A tropical cyclone is named when it is judged to have 10-minute sustained windspeeds of 65&#160;km/h (40&#160;mph).<sup id="cite_ref-172" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-172">[171]</a></sup> The JMA selected the names from a list of 140 names, that had been developed by the 14 members nations and territories of the <a href="/wiki/List_of_retired_Pacific_typhoon_names#Background" title="List of retired Pacific typhoon names">ESCAP/WMO Typhoon Committee</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-Retired_typhoons_173-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Retired_typhoons-173">[172]</a></sup> Retired names, if any, will be announced by the <a href="/wiki/World_Meteorological_Organization" title="World Meteorological Organization">WMO</a> in 2018; though replacement names will be announced in 2019. The next 28&#160;names on the naming list are listed here along with their international numeric designation, if they are used. During the season the names Hato and Lan were used for the first time, after it replaced the names <a href="/wiki/Tropical_Storm_Washi" title="Tropical Storm Washi">Washi</a> and <a href="/wiki/Typhoon_Vicente" title="Typhoon Vicente">Vicente</a>, which was retired after the <a href="/wiki/2011_Pacific_typhoon_season" title="2011 Pacific typhoon season">2011</a> and <a href="/wiki/2012_Pacific_typhoon_season" title="2012 Pacific typhoon season">2012 seasons</a>.</p>\n<table style="width:100%;">\n<tr>\n<td>\n<ul>\n<li>Muifa (1701)</li>\n<li>Merbok (1702)</li>\n<li>Nanmadol (1703)</li>\n<li>Talas (1704)</li>\n<li>Noru (1705)</li>\n<li>Kulap (1706)</li>\n<li>Roke (1707)</li>\n</ul>\n</td>\n<td>\n<ul>\n<li>Sonca (1708)</li>\n<li>Nesat (1709)</li>\n<li>Haitang (1710)</li>\n<li>Nalgae (1711)</li>\n<li>Banyan (1712)</li>\n<li>Hato (1713)</li>\n<li>Pakhar (1714)</li>\n</ul>\n</td>\n<td>\n<ul>\n<li>Sanvu (1715)</li>\n<li>Mawar (1716)</li>\n<li>Guchol (1717)</li>\n<li>Talim (1718)</li>\n<li>Doksuri (1719)</li>\n<li>Khanun (1720)</li>\n<li>Lan (1721)</li>\n</ul>\n</td>\n<td>\n<ul>\n<li><b>Saola (1722)&#160;<i>(active)</i></b></li>\n<li><span style="color:#666666">Damrey&#160;<i>(unused)</i></span></li>\n<li><span style="color:#666666">Haikui&#160;<i>(unused)</i></span></li>\n<li><span id="Philippines">Philippines</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2017_Pacific_typhoon_season&amp;action=edit&amp;section=36" title="Edit section: Philippines">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">Main article: <a href="/wiki/List_of_retired_Philippine_typhoon_names" title="List of retired Philippine typhoon names">List of retired Philippine typhoon names</a></div>\n<p>This season, PAGASA will use its own naming scheme for cyclones, that will either develop within or move into their self-defined area of responsibility.<sup id="cite_ref-PAGASA_Names_174-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PAGASA_Names-174">[173]</a></sup> The names were taken from a list of names, that was last used during <a href="/wiki/2013_Pacific_typhoon_season" title="2013 Pacific typhoon season">2013</a> and are scheduled to be used again during 2021.<sup id="cite_ref-PAGASA_Names_174-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PAGASA_Names-174">[173]</a></sup> All of the names are the same except for Lannie, Salome and Yasmin, which replaced the names <a href="/wiki/Typhoon_Utor" title="Typhoon Utor">Labuyo</a>, <a href="/wiki/Typhoon_Nari_(2013)" title="Typhoon Nari (2013)">Santi</a> and <a href="/wiki/Typhoon_Haiyan" title="Typhoon Haiyan">Yolanda</a> after they were retired.<sup id="cite_ref-PAGASA_Names_174-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PAGASA_Names-174">[173]</a></sup> The name Lannie was used for the first time this year.</p>\n<table class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2017_Pacific_typhoon_season&amp;action=edit&amp;section=39" title="Edit section: Notes">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>\n<div class="reflist" style="list-style-type: decimal;">\n<div class="mw-references-wrap">\n<ol class="references">\n<li id="cite_note-9"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-9">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">The totals represent the sum of the squares for every (sub)tropical storm\'s intensity of over 33&#160;knots (38&#160;mph, 61&#160;km/h), divided by 10,000. Calculations are provided at <a href="/wiki/Talk:2017_Pacific_typhoon_season/ACE_calcs" title="Talk:2017 Pacific typhoon season/ACE calcs">Talk:2017 Pacific typhoon season/ACE calcs</a>.</span></li>\n<li id="cite_note-SouthChina-175"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-SouthChina_175-0">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">South China includes the provinces of <a href="/wiki/Hainan" title="Hainan">Hainan</a>, <a href="/wiki/Guangxi" title="Guangxi">Guangxi</a>, <a href="/wiki/Guangdong" title="Guangdong">Guangdong</a>, <a href="/wiki/Hong_Kong" title="Hong Kong">Hong Kong</a> and <a href="/wiki/Macau" title="Macau">Macau</a></span></li>\n<li id="cite_note-Indochina-178"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-Indochina_178-0">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">Indochina is an area in <a href="/wiki/Southeast_Asia" title="Southeast Asia">Southeast Asia</a> which includes <a href="/wiki/Vietnam" title="Vietnam">Vietnam</a>, <a href="/wiki/Cambodia" title="Cambodia">Cambodia</a>, <a href="/wiki/Laos" title="Laos">Laos</a>, <a href="/wiki/Malaysia" title="Malaysia">Malaysia</a>, <a href="/wiki/Myanmar" title="Myanmar">Myanmar</a> and <a href="/wiki/Thailand" title="Thailand">Thailand</a></span></li>\n</ol>\n</div>\n</div>\n<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="References">References</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2017_Pacific_typhoon_season&amp;action=edit&amp;section=40" title="Edit section: References">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>\n<div class="reflist columns references-column-width" style="-moz-column-width: 30em;
